ched gnyer gsol ba btab nas g.yag TIka rin chen bang mdzod kyi lung yang thob gsung/der bka' chos de rnams grol rjes/ rje rdo rje 'chang gis/ srad/ seng ge rtse/ dpal
ldan sa skya'i bar du/ bla ma sde dpon so so la 'bul sdud kyi bka' shog 'thems pa stsal zhing/ da drung nas slob dpon pa rnams sngon la byon/ nged kyang glo bo nas 'bod mi
'dug pas/ rjes la sleb yong bas nged gang 'dug tu byon mdzod// ces pa'i bka' lung bzhin sngon la phyin/ de rjes phyag dam la brten 'bul sdud kyang dpe bral byung zhing/
zla gcig tsam song dus chu 'dus tshor/ rje dpon slob rnams phebs zer ba thos nas/ zhabs drung du bsnyags/ der zla ba phyed tsam gdan chags shing/ de ring tshogs la zhen
pa gzhi bral gyi khrid gsung ba/ nged shar phyogs nas yongs pa'i dpon slob kun gyis zhus shing/ der rje'i phyag phyir byon 'dug pas/ khwa char byang chub sems dpa'i drung
du/ gzungs chen grwa lnga dang/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar can/ lha mangs gnyis ka'i dbang dang/ lha mo 'od zer can lha lnga'i dbang/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho'i drung
du seng ge sgra rje btsun

bsod nams rtse mo'i yig cha'i steng nas rjes gnang/ gdon dgrol dkar shAka/ dmar chos rgyal/ gdung brgyud rin rgyal rnams kyis mdzad pa'i lung yang/ chu 'dus pa'i sde pa zhal
ngo'i zla la rdo rje 'chang chen pos bka' stsal gnang nas thob/ der rdo rje 'chang gis 'bul sdud la phan pa'i dngos pa'i gnang sbyin bsam gyis mi khyab pa dag dang/ khwa
char byang chub sems dpa'/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho ba gnyis kyis kyang rje rong chen pa'i dgongs rdzogs la dmigs pa'i der 'bul ba byung ba kun stsal/ sems dpa'
chen po legs pa'i shes rab drung la/ de dus gnang rgyu cher mi snang yang/ mnga' ris phyogs nas dge bskul dang bcas bgyid ces brtse ba'i thugs dungs yang dag snang/ de rjes
dpon slob yongs kyis thugs brtse ba lhung ba de'i mthus/ spyir sde pa chu 'dus pas gnang sbyin dpag med dang/ lhag par chu 'dus mkhas btsun pa'i drung gis snam bem skyer
kha snam bu gang zhig la de bas legs pa rang res gyon ma myong gsung ba'i na bza' dpe bral/ des gtsos pa'i 'bul ba gnang sbyin yang dag stsal zhing/ de lta'i na bza'
de ni phyis gser mdog can gyi chos 'khor chen mo mdzad dus kyang sku la gsol zhing/ de rjes glo bo chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan pa la mnga' ris la phebs dus stsal nas/
ding sang bdag pa'i mchod zhing du mnga' ris na bzhugs so//der rdo rje 'chang gi bka' lung la/ da res gsang phu'i dus mchod gtong ba sogs la byon/ glo bo nas kyang dus mchod
rang gi stengs su mi 'byor bapa 'dug kyang/ dgun chos stengs su mang ja 'gyed bcas kyi skul 'debs byed/ nged mnga' ris su lo ngo gsum tsam las mi thogs pas slar ngor
tshor sleb

pa gsan skabs byon/ chos 'phro sogs yong ba bgyid sogs kyi bslab ston dang/ mar phyogs kyi sde pa so sor yang 'bul sdud la phan pa'i bka' shog lam yig stsal zhes/ 'di dag chu
'dus pa dbang phyug gi ngag las dngos kyis thos so//gsang sngags rab 'byams slob mkhas gong ma'i mdun//ji bzhin mkhas par bslabs khyod khengs min la//rang blo yig ngor
drangs pa'i mkhas 'dod can//smra brjod mkhan de glu mkhan gzhogs 'phya'i tshul//rong ston bstan pa'i nyi ma nub kyi spor//mdzad pa'i rjes mthar yongs su nub nas slar//khyod
sku dge mtshan bya ba'i 'od dkris can//legs smon shar gyi ri rtser lhang nger gsal//rig 'dzin 'chi med mchog brnyes grub pa'i rje//drang srong bgres po'i spyan sngar
rgan po'i ngag//phyis 'byung byis pa'i bla brjod ma 'dres pa'i//sngon rabs chos kyi ro bcud tshim par bzhes//tshul gnas dri bsung 'phro ba'i mkhan po mchog//zhi dul sbyangs
pa'i gnas brtan dam pa'i drung//ji skad bshad pa'i las grwa dpe bral las//gang khyod bsnyen par rdzogs zhes gtam du gleng//'dul ba rgya mtsho'i pha rol mthar phyin zhing//gnang
bkag khrims brgya'i nges gnas nor bu'i mdzod//'dul 'dzin 'bum sde'i ded dpon zla bral khyod//gsol bzhi'i las kyi sgyu thabs len 'di mtshar//rang bzhin khrims kyi
lus gtsang dri ma med//bag yod shes bzhin gos mchog 'dzin pa can//mkhas slob las kyi cho ga'i mig 'phrul la//ci nas brten 'di dam chos sgyu ma'i gar//zhes paNDi ta chen
po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i skabs las bsgrags

pa'i rab tu byed pa dgu pa'o//Chapter 10: gsang phur dge tshogs rgya cher spel ba'i skabsder 'bul sdud kyi dngos gnas rnams zhu phyir mar lam rje don yod dpal ba dpon slob
rnams/ span khyung tshang na bzhugs pa'i drung du byon pas dges dges dpag med dang/ na ning skyor mo lung tshor bsdad dus slob dpon 'ga' khang pa'i gsung gis/ mkhan chen
chos skyabs pas rnam sras lus dang grib ma bzhin du 'brang gsung/ gnas sgo slob dpon pa la thugs mthong che zer dus/ 'chams sku gog po dkon gnyer gyis drung?drud pa'i nyams
cig las ma byung/ da 'a rdzi rdzi ba 'dug go//nged kyis kun mkhyen sga gdong pa la tshe dbang dang/ bkra shis tshe ring ma'i dbang gsol ba btab nas zhal gyis bzhes yod
pas ming de'i don khyed la ldan dgos pa a pho rgan po dang lhan cig zhu ba lags so gsung/ nged la skyel thung gi tshul du rin chen gling bar phebs/ rje'i drung dang mchod
yon thugs snang dag par 'dug cing/ dad mos lhag par che ba gnang bas/ nged dpon slob gsar rnying yos/ nang pa'i nang der gnas tshang byas/ de'i ya tshad kyi jo mo dgon
chung chud der/ kun mkhyen sga dgong pa bzhugs pa gnang ba'i sar nged dpon slob dang/ rin chen gling nang pa rnam pas phyin/ ma pham g.yag pa las chos rje gzhon nu seng ge
bas gsan/ de la kun mkhyen sga dgong pa rang gis gsan pa'i tshe dpag med grub pa'i rgyal mo'i tshe dbang dang/ bkra shis tshe rings mched lnga'i rjes gnang byung zhing/
de'i skabs nam zla dpyid sos kyang gangs thul tsam babs pas kun mkhyen sga gdong pa'i gsung gis/ khyed dpon slob la tshe rings ma 'go bar snang gsung zhing/ de dus kun mkhyen
sga dgong pa sku chas jo gdan chos lung pa'i lugs kyi phrag dbyung ma/ de'i phyi la snam stod?stong dur kha dar ljang gis mtha' chag byas pa zhig dang

dbu zhwa paN zhwa dmar po sna rings cig gsol 'dug pas/ nged der 'dus kyi slob dpon yo 'ga' re sku chas kyi rnam pa'i tshul 'ga' re gtor ma tshe rings ma'i gdas gtor yin zer
ba'i ri 'dra ba la mar gyis byil byil byas pa 'dug pa la/ 'ga' re rol mo'i chas rdung ba'i rnam 'gyur sogs rgyu mtshan ma nges pa so so nas rgad cha che ba re byung ba ci'i
rten 'brel yin ni ma nges gsung zhes rnal 'byor dbu legs grub chen pa'i gsung sgros la sogs brgyud pa'o//der gsang phu tsho 'di la rang mos 'brel che zhes/ bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa'i thugs dam zab khyad rngog lo tsa ba blo ldan shes rab nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dbyangs gang blo ma'i bstod bsgrub 'od zer dgu phrugs ma de yang/ nged shar
nas 'ongs pa'i dpon slob rnams la stsal/ de nas mar lam gzhis ka rin spungs nas/ ngur smrig gi rje btsun sgrol ma dang mjal/ dpal sde la byas nas mar lam nyes skyon gtan
med par gsang phur phyin zhing/ dbyar chos kyi dus mchod stengs su ja phogs/ skam 'gyed sogs sngon med kyi srol rgya cher gtod pa'i dus mchod bzang dpe la 'khyer ba rang
re'i bsam pa snying nas tshim pa byung zhing/ spyir gsang phu'i slob dpon tsho la dus mchod ma thongs bar phrin las cher mi yong zhing/ dus mchod legs pa re thongs rjes
'bad med lhun grub yong ba zhig yod pa ltar/ rang re la yang dus mchod de thongs phyin/ grwa pa rnams la'ang na tsha shi chad dkon pa dang/ kha ton slob gnyer 'phel nges
byung bas/ 'phrang po nyi ma phug/ skyor mo lung/ gung thang/ mkhar rtse/ nA lendra/ glang thang/ chos sdings/ rgya ma sogs nges med du 'pho skyas la brten pa'i 'chad nyan
snying non pa rang byung zhes 'phros so//der dus mchod de thongs rjes nA lendrar phebs pas de

dus rje rong chen gyi nang rten thub dbang dang/ dngul gdung gi rab gnas la bdag po mthu stobs dbang phyug zha lu ba bsod nams rgyal ba spyan drangs 'dug pa'i rab gnas grol
rjes nged chos sleb/ der khong dag gi skyor zlos la mar lam rdzong dkar du kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel bas spyan drangs/ der rong phyogs na brag khyung mgo sdig pa 'dra
ba/ skyed tshal gyi chos grwa la sa dgra che ba zhig yod pa la/ gtor ma gtad nas 'phangs pa'i de ma thag brag ral nas byung zer ba dang/ zhag lnga drug cig gi gong tsam
du nA lendra rang du thog byung ba sdigs mdzub kyis bskor/ shing sdong gdags gzhi can zhig yod pa la brgyab pa dngos gsal du phebs pas dad mos kyis sems drangs nas kye rdor
rgyu dbang/ gur lha brgyad/ khyad par zhal bzhi pa'i bsnyen bsgrub las gsum/ spags chog bram ze'i rig gtad dang lnga'i rjes gnang bsgrub skor rnams zhus shing/ de'i dgun
klu gong phyogs su de'i rgyal pos gnod 'tshe cher byung ba/ nA lendra nas chos rje dgas po ba'i sku chos kyis bcings pa la sta gri bsnun pas/ shing sdong la khrag shor
zhing/ dam la dngos su thogs/ de'i snyan pas dbus gong ma'i thugs la rgya 'dra'i tshang bcas lo mang po song/ dbus phyogs kyi bla ma nus che che mo mang pos btul kyang gtan
glags ma phye ba la/ chos rje pa nA lendra nas spyan drangs zhag bcur bsten/ de dang chos 'bel gtam gnang skad cing/ mthar kho nyid rgya gar du paNDi ta buddha bha dra
bya bar skye ba bzung rgol ba sogs gsal por zhus/ zhabs spyi bor nod nas phyir thon/ gong ma chen mo sku khams sor chud rjes 'bul ba zhabs 'degs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang
bcas byon pa'i tshur lam/ nged gsang phu'i dgun chos la 'gro ba dang ram sgang du mjal bas yid spro ba byung nas/ rje rang gi thugs dam phyag

na rdo rje 'byung po kun 'dul gyi rjes gnang zhig zhu zhes zhu ba gnang bas/ chos rje dgas po'i gsung gis/ de ka byed byin rlabs kyi rgyun brtan par yod gsung dges bzhin du
stsal/ de phyin chad bsgom bzlas ma chag par byas shing/ hUM badzra phaT 'dis cho phye ba zhig yin gsung nas/ drin can spyang lung pa'i bka' 'brel gsan pa'i thog ma rang
yin pas de ltar gsung zhes bdag cag la bka' stsal to//de'i lo dgun chos stengs su mnga' ris glo bo nas/ nang chen dpal drung btsan zhes pas mgo byas pa'i gsang phur mang
ja bskol ba la gnang ba kun gyis lam bde ba kho nas legs par brtol te/ der mang ja zhag sbrel mang po dang/ dza ti/ ras sngo dmar so ba 'ga' byi sogs stod rdzas kyis tshogs
la spyi 'gyed bzang po/ mkhan slob rnams la dgongs ja bu ram stengs su shel ka ra/ rgyal mo ka ra/ bye ma ka ra/ rgun 'bum sogs shing 'bras rnam grangs mang po/ rgya
gar nas 'ongs pa'i dge slong gis bsten rung kha na ma tho ba med pa'i bsnyen bkur blo 'das/ zangs/ gser/ byi ru spos shel/ mu tig sogs kyi 'bul ba gya nom pa sngon chad mthong
thos kyi yul du ma gyur ba'i zab rgyas dpag med byung/ der lo rgyus mkhan po 'dus pa'i dbus su paN chen rin po che nyid kyis gnang nas/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa spyi dang
khyad par dagvc: or: ngag?las brtsams te/ snyan ngag gi tshigs su bcad pa spel legs ngang pa'i sgra dang/ bung ba'i dbyangs ltar rjes su sgrog par mdzad pas der 'dus pa
kun dang/ khyad par mnga' ris pa'i mos dge can de dag gis/ sngon chad rna ba'i rgyan char ma blangs pa'i legs bshad utpa la'i phreng ba gsar pa dag gis yid dbang lhag par
phrogs/ snying nas dad pa'i spu lang long du rgya cher g.yos par gyur te rang rang gi rgyan du btags pa'i spos shel gyi zhags pa yid du

'ong zhing rin gzhal dka' ba dag kyang rdos phangs pa med par cham chos du brdungs nas spos dud sbyangs te dad pa'i mig chu'i yon chab kyis bzhin ras kyi me tog brgyan par
byas nas 'dus pa'i tshogs de dag la gus par bstabs so//der yongs pa'i dge ba'i las can de dag slar rang yul du lam gyi 'jigs pa gang gis kyang ma reg par son par gyur tshe/
dngos gnas kyi tshul de dag rgya cher sgrog cing/ lhag par snyan ngag gi tshig 'bru gsar pa'i yi ge dag/ glo bo sde pa tshangs chen bkra shis mgon po'i spyan lam du phebs
pas dges pa rab dang mchog gi rtser byon zhes grags shing/ de dus kyi snyan ngag gi tshig sdebs legs su bsgrigs pa'i cha tsam zhig brjod na/'dzam bu'i sgra yis mtshon
pa yi//zhing 'di mdzes pa'i rgyan drug dang//spyod pa'i brtul zhugs grub pa yis//'phags yul bdud rtsi'i lam chen gtod//ces rgya gar du dam pa'i chos rgyas shing dar tshul/rmongs
pa'i khang bur yun ring du//mi shes nad kyis gzir ba yi//gangs khrod mun pa'i snag rum 'dir//lo paN chos kyi nyi mas bskyangs//zhes bod yul du sangs rgyas kyi bstan
pa rin po che 'phel tshul/smon lam grub pa'i rgyal sras ni//padmo can dang 'jam dbyangs dang//kun gyi yab gyur kun bzang gis//'gro 'di'i bde skyid yun rings bzung//zhes
chos rgyal mes dbon rnam gsum gyi sku ring la bstan pa snga dar gyi byung tshul/mda' lnga ldan pa'i snying stobs kyis//'byung po'i dpung tshogs kun bsdus nas//dus mthar
rgyal ngan glang chen gyis//rmongs pa'i dug gis nyer gtses mod//ces glang dar gyis bstan pa bsnubs tshul/de tshe der yang dge blo can//sems dpa' snying stobs chen pos ni//mthu
stobs

ye shes snang ba yis//mun pa'i klong chen skad cig bsal//zhes lha lung dpal gyi rdo rjes glang dar bsgral tshul/thub pa'i bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs//snyigs ma lnga la brtser
dgongs nas//nyi ma'i gnyen gyi gdung 'dzin pa'i//ye shes 'od ces bya ba 'khrungs//lta ngan bon gyi gzhung lugs dang//sbyor sgrol chos su sgrog pa'i ngag//skal dman mu stegs
gzhogs 'phya ba'i//spyod pa'i lam ngan dengs par mdzad//ces bstan pa phyi dar gyi dbu brtsams tshul/de nas mnga' ris kun da'i gnyen//lo chen sgrib bral zla ba dang//byang
phyogs pad tshal 'byed pa'i lha//blo ldan smra ba'i nyi ma bltams//zhes lo chen rin bzang dang/ rngog blo ldan shes rab byon tshul/dus der 'chad rtsod rtsom pa dang//thub
bstan rin chen 'dzin pa'i phul//'jig rten mig gyur lo tsa bas//kha ba can ljongs yongs su khyab//ces 'brog/ 'gos/ mar pa lo tsa sogs bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dpag med
byon tshul/dus 'dir nges par mi'i dbang po//tshangs pa bzhin du dge ba dang//dpal dang 'byor pa phun sum tshogs//bkra shis dpal gyi mgon po des//ces sbyin bdag gi nges
gnas kyi tshul/sa stengs 'di na 'gran med cing//skya rengs bu ltar grags pa'i tog//srid rtse'i bar du bsgreng mkhas pa'i//bstan pa'i ring lugs nye bar bzung//zhes sa skya
pa'i bstan pa'i sbyin gnas mchog tu bzhugs tshul/dpal ldan sa skya'i rig 'dzin dbang//kun dga'i chos kyi 'khor lo bsgyur//bla na med pa'i don stsol ba//'dod dgu'i dpag
bsam bzang po rnyed//ces khyad par de dus rdo rje 'chang spyan drangs pa'i skabs mtshon tshul rnams tshig nyung zhing don mang ba/ sdebs legs pa'i legs par bshad pas thugs
mchog

tu dges te/ da ni 'di lta bu'i bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu dam pa 'di/ sa 'dir spyan ci nas 'drongs par byas nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i rgyun/ rgya chen
po dar zhing rgyas pa'i bya ba bsgrub pa nyid la nan tan du bgyid do// zhes thugs kyi yul du dgongs nas yang nas yang du gsung byon pa yin/ zhes de dus kyi zhabs 'bring
dag cig gi ngag nas gleng ngo//der gsang phu'i dgun chos grol nas/ 'phrang phu'i dpyid chos ma tshugs bar du grwa thang du phebs nas/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan pa'i drung
du tshad ma rigs pa'i gter rang 'grel dang bcas pa 'u yug pa'i rigs mdzod dang sbyar ba'i zab bshad nyid legs par gsan zhing/ der chos rje shes rab zla ba sogs kyis zhus
pa'i zla la/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dbang/ rnal 'byor bzhi'i khrid kyang gsan no//de mtshams 'phrang phur dpyid chos la phebs/ de grol rjes 'phrang phu na tha snyad kyis
paN chen rin po che nyid kyi a ner mtshon pa'i 'phrang phu ba'i yum bgres mo zhig bzhugs pa des bslab bya mdzad pa ni/ drung nas khyed la sku tshe ring ba cig pus chog
par snang bas/ tshe bsgrub rang la 'bungs mdzod cig/ sku tshe ring na de bar la da lta'i 'gran tshol rang mnyam yo rdzogs nas/ 'gran zla kun bral gyi bstan pa'i bya ba
rlabs can rang 'bad med du mdzad rgyu yod pas/ rang re bod 'dra ba'i gdams ngag 'di kun la zungs shig rang mi snang/ na ning shed 'di na mar la/ paNDi ta shA ri'i pu tro
bya ba dgung lo brgya tsam lon nges yin zer/ 'phral ni dgung lo lnga bcu nga bgrang tsam 'gro ba'i tshod cig 'dug/ khong kun la 'chi med grub pa bya ba'i gdams pa bzhugs
zer na'ang/ de kun ni khams la byas rgya nag rgyal pos spyan drangs song zer/ da lta yang bsam yas na rgya gar gyi paNDi ta nags

kyi rin chen zer ba'i mkhas pa las kyang grub pa gtso che ba zhig bzhugs yod par 'dug cing/ paNDi ta de rang ra'i kun mkhyen rong pos nga'i lo bdun gyi gong de la/ drang srong
srin po ri'i bde mchog pho brang du/ mi g.yo bla med sogs kyi dbang gsan pa'i bla ma yang yin pas/ paNDi ta de'i drung du byon la/ khong la rgya gar gyi slob dpon ngag
gi dbang phyug dngos kyis gnang ba'i sgrol dkar gyi tshe grub bzhugs zer bas de zhus mdzod/ rgya gar ba bya ba rten 'brel brtag dpyad che zhing/ gser la gtsigs su che bas
'di dag phul zer sngon gyi bkra shis kha thags/ sgo tshad ma gsar pa dri ma med pa cig dang/ gser zho gsum byin/ lam gyi rta dang chas sogs kyang bskur nas/ chu byang
la byas phyin pas/ paN chen nags rin bsam yas kyi byang chub chen po'i drung na bzhugs pa dang mjal/ der lo tsa ba mnga' ris pa yin zer ba'i manydzu ba zer ba zhig 'dug pa
la zhu ba bskur bas/ mjal kha de 'phral rang la byung/ khong gis bskur ba'i bkra shis kha thags bzang po de phyag mjal la phul bas/ 'dzum mdzad nas mahA tsin gyi pa To
la gsung phyag tu bzhes so//de lo tsa ba des rgya nag gi dar dkar po yin gsung zer bsgyur byung/ de 'phral chos 'brel thog ma gyis gsung rnam 'joms dang mtshan brjod rgya
skad du lung stsal/ de'i sang nyid shar la byang chub chen po'i drung du/ sbu tshal ba'i sku ngo rnams bsnyen nas zhu ba la byon gsung/ khong dag la bsnyen gnas kyi bslab
ston stsal rjes/ nged la lo tsa ba de brgyud nas khyed rten gang yin gsung/ dge slong yin zhus pas/ 'o nang par gzhan la ster dgos/ nga yang sde pa thams cad yod smra ka
yin gsung/ brgyud pa gsungs pa'i klu sgrub yan yongs grags 'di kar 'dug/ der saM skRa ta'i skad du lung stsal/ der lo tsa ba

manydzu ba la/ rang gi 'dod kyi grol dkar tshe bsgrub de zhus pas/ kho na re/ paNDi ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang dus kyang mi mtshungs/ dngos su gsan pa'i rgyu med/ sngar mi
ma tshor zhus pas chog zer zhus byung bas/ zhal 'dzum mdzad nged rang la bod du 'di dgos zer ba kho gcig pu las ma byung na'ang/ bar du lo tsa ni byed du mi btub/ khos ni
nga'i skad mi go'am gsung phebs pa'i bka' lung byung bas/ der nged kyis kha rtsang gnang ba'i rgya skad rnams legs par go//saM skRa ta'i skad cung zad shes zhus pas/ paN
chen nags rin dges nas drung du bos/ rgya gar gyi skad du 'dri mal gnang ba'i lan 'debs rim par phul bas/ sad ta sad ta gsung zhing/ der gser zho gsum po phul nas tshe
bsgrub khyad par can de yang zhus/ dges pa'i sgo nas stsal zhing/ phyag dpe ka lA pa'i sgra mdo'i po ti zhig kyang gnang ba yang da lta'i bar yang lag na yod do//phyis gos
sku g.yed can 'grub pa dang/ tshe la bar chad med pa paNDi ta de la bkra shis kha thags phul ba dang/ tshe bsgrub ngo mtshar can thob pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug gsung zhes
legs par rtogs so// 'di thad zur tsam rnam thar rdor rgyal ma na bris snang ngo//mkhyen yang blo gros rab rgyas sprin gyi rnga//snyan par bsgrags pas rma bya gzhon nu'i
yid//dga' ba'i mdongs mtha' rgyas pa ngoms byed cing//yi rangs gar gyi zlas gar ci yang bsgyur//dpyod ldan yongs kyi tshad ma'i dpang gyur te//'jigs med smra ba'i dbang por
mtshan gsol ba//gang la rtsad cing dris pa'i don 'di rnams//yid la re ba'i 'bras stsol a shwa tha//tshul gnas mang thos zhi dul bag yod tshul//mthong bas rab mgu gus pa'i
spu long dag//'bad med g.yo ba'i rang bzhin las 'ongs pa'i//zang zing yon gyi sbyin gnas mchog tu bkur//dkon nor dpag yas 'dus pa'i dge 'dun la//dang ba'i shugs kyis
bstabs nas dge tshogs dag//mtha' yas 'gro la sbyin mdzad

khyod kyi thugs//rab tu dges pas tshim ste dal bar bzhugs//chos sbyin bsam yas lhar bcas 'gro ba'i yid//yongs drangs zang zing mi 'jigs byams pas bskyangs//phan dang bde ba'i
dpal la 'god pa'i gnyen//lus can yongs kyi ma 'dris mdza' bshes mchog//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam
par 'byed pa las/ gsang phur dge tshogs rgya cher spel ba'i skabs las bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa bcu pa'o// //Chapter 11: gdan sa chen por gzhung lugs rab 'byams kyi
ngag rjes su sgrogs pa'i skabsder paN chen rin po che dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdunrtsa bdun du phebs pa shing pho khyi lo'i vc: 1454dbyar chos stengs su thugs rtsom che ba
rnams kyi thog ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dka' 'grel bzhed tshul rgya mtsho'i rlabs kyi phreng ba'i thugs rtsom yang gnang zhing/ de gong du yang lus dang yan
lag rgyas par bshad pa lung don rgya mtsho/ sbyor TIka gnad kyi sgron me sogs rong TIka nyid kyi dgongs len ji lta ba'i bstan bcos phran bu ba dag gis kyang gdul bya'i zhe
'dod kyi re ba yongs su rdzogs par mdzad la/ gzhan yang mtshon byed dpe'i dge 'dun gyi zur 'debs ngag gi dbang po'i mdzes rgyan/ bsam gzugs kyi zur 'debs ngag gi dbang
po'i do shal/ rten 'brel gyi zur 'debs srid zhi'i gnas tshul 'char byed rnams kyang rnam bshad tshig don rab gsal nyid dang rjes 'brel yin no//dgung lo nyer bdun gyi skabs
kyi ston chag la yang grwa tshang chos sdings su zla ba nyis sbrel tsam gyi phogs 'bul mi byung nas phebs/ de dus spyang lung rin po che'i drung na byang sems bde mo thang
pa dpon slob 'ga' la thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid grub thob tshem bu ba nas brgyud pa de gnang ba'i dbu tshugs tsam la sleb nas nged grwa tshang pa kun gyis zhus/
de grol rjes ri bo dge ldan pa'i

dge bshes/ phyis dkar brgyud du phyogs pa sha ra rab 'byams pa sang rgyas seng ge bas zhu ba'i gtso byas nas/ 'bri stag/ 'brug pa stod smad/ karma zhwa dmar nag gnyis ka'i
brgyud pa tshang ba'i nA ro chos drug dang/ phyag rgya chen po spyan snga bsod nams rgyal mtshan pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig ma rig mun sel du grags pa de'i steng nas lhan cig
skyes sbyor/ yang dgon pa'i ri chos skor gsum gyi lung sogs dang/ yang de grol rjes rang chos rje sher 'byung blo gros sbas pa zhes bya (ba)?zhu ba'i ri bo dge ldan pa'i
grub thob chen po rang du grags pa des zhus nas/ nai gu'i khrid tshar gcig kyang thob cing/ snga phyir ne gu lan bzhi zhus zhes paN chen rin po che nyid kyi slob ma mnga'
ris su byon pa'i bsgrub pa'i brgyud 'dzin gcig pu ba/ khog lung rab 'byams pa nam mkha' rab gsal ba'i zhal nas brgyud pa'i gsung sgros so//der spyang lung rin po che'i
drung du bka' chos gsan rjes/ glang thang spyan snga kun rdor ba sku mched kyis spyan 'dren rkang btsugs byung nas/ glang ri 'od ldan du phebs pas bka' lung la gtsang phyogs
nas mgron po yong ba'i skad cha la/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang chen po mnga' ris glo bo 'khor nas ngor tshor phebs yod 'dug pas sngon zhal bzhes bzang po yod pa'i don
la rkang gtad gtsang phyogs la 'byon par rigs gsung/ der rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung du zhu yig/ rten gos bem lu haM ri mo me tog zlum 'dzings ma cig dang/ gnang sbyin
chos zhu ba'i chas la phan pa'i ja gos dar dpag med stsal nas/ dgun grang ba'i sgang rang yin na'ang blos longs pa byas/ tshal pa rin rgyal ba dang khra phu ba sangs
rgyas bzang pos gtso mdzad pa'i grwa pa slob gnyer ba mthar phyin lung rigs brda sbyangs pa rang drag bsdus dang bcas gtsang phyogs su phebs

shing/ de yang thog mar rje don yod dpal ba dpon slob rnams pan khyung tshang na bzhugs pa'i drung du thegs/ der yab sras zhal mjal ma thag dges dges mtha' yas rang gnang zhing/
zhag 'ga' re'i gong du ngor tshor phebs/ rdo rje 'chang dang mjal ba'i gsung sgros dang/ da rdo rje 'chang yang spyan kyang rab rib tu song/ sku na tshod mthar phyin
pa'i stabs bka' chos zhu ba'i skabs rang na 'dug/ nyi ma gangs thogs tu phebs zer ba'i dper gda'o gsung//der paN chen rin po che'i thugs dgongs la rje rdo rje 'chang dgung
lo bdun cu don bzhir phebs pa yin kyang/ spyang lung rin po che dgung lo brgyad cu gya bzhi bzhes pa yang/ spyan gsal/ snyan sang/ ljags bde/ sku lus bskyod pa yang/
bka' chos nyin rangs stsol yang dub pa mi mnga' ba 'dug pa snyam pa byung yang de'i phyi lo rang rje rdo rje 'chang zhing khams brje ba gnang song zhing/ rang re'i rje don
yod dpal ba'i bka' lung 'di kun ma 'ongs mngon mkhyen rang du yod// ces paN chen dngos la chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas gsan pa'i gsung sgros so//der dgun chos kyi
brngod 'thag sogs la zhag 'ga' chags pas/ ngor tshor sleb dus snang gsum gyi dag pa'i snang ba de non tsam byung zhing/ der sems bskyed sngags lam man dang/ sngar ma thob
pa'i lam 'bras kyi cha lag rnams dang/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa rnams byung/ der rang re'i grogs rnams pas gros 'debs da res gtsang la phebs pa la dpal ldan sa skyar grwa
skor cig gnang ba legs zer byung ba la/ rang res de 'dra'i shes 'dod kyang med/ gsang phu'i las 'dzin 'di'i stabs dang/ da res chos zhu ba la rang rkang gtad pa'i g.yeng
bar 'gyur bas mi byed byas thag bcad pas/ khong chos rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung du tshul phul nas/ der bka' lung

la/ spyir sa skya pa'i dge bshes su 'jog pa la gdan sa chen por bstan pa'i rnam gzhag re nges par gnang ba srol du 'dug cing/ khyed lta bu'i mkhyen rab yod pas grwa skor cig
gnang na ma 'ongs pa'i mig ltos la yang phan pas cis kyang mdzod// ces bkas bskul tshul rnam thar rje dbon ma ti ma las 'byung zhing/ 'di skabs de gnyis ka dang gzhan dag
gi snyun na mi bzhugs pa'i khyad par ba'i brjod pa dag cig rnam thar rdor rgyal mar bris pa ni/ khong gi bka' dang rjes 'brel/ sngon der grwa skor cig gi bzhed pa yod
kyang/ sngags phyogs la 'dun pas mdo'i slob gnyer tsam ma 'grub pas ma byung/ da de'i tshab tu dmigs nas khyod kyis mdzod ces/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi na bza' ngur samaRag
tshon ldan gyi dbu zhwa nas zhabs lham yan gyi gnang sbyin gnang bas der paN chen rin po ches/ bka' bzhin grwa skor bsgrub par zhu/ bla ma'i na bza' 'a res gar longs
spyod spobs zhes bzhugs sar bla re gnang ba gsan nas/ yang sngar lta bu'i ngur smrig tshon ldan gsar pa cha gcig gnang nas/ sngar de nged kyis gyon pas khyed mi bsnoms
na 'di bzhes mdzod ces bka' lung gnang zhes 'byung ngo//der bka' lung la/ grwa pa rnams pan rang du slob dpon pa'i rtsar btang na khong rang rnam pa yang dpe cha 'dra gtong
ba'i khyad 'dra yang yong bas de lugs dang/ 'di nas rang yang de ring sku mtshams kyi mu nas phyag dpe gzigs pa la nan tan mdzod// phyag dpe gang dgos dge slong pa'i lag
nas bzhes pas khyab gsung ba la/ grwa pa rnams bka' bzhin pan khyung tshang rang du rdzong zhing/ dpe cha lta mi dgos pa yod lags shing/ da res chos zhu rang la bsnyags
pa yin pas/ bka' chos gang rgyas rang gi sku drin dgos zhu ba gnang yang/ rdo rje 'chang gi bka' lung

la sa skya'i grwa skor 'di bla ma gong ma'i byin rlabs kyi zil dang byas dka' ba rang zhig yod pas/ phyag dpe gzigs pa'i sku mtshams dam pa rang mdzod/ gsung chos ma gsan pa
'dra yod na brda 'bul gsung/ der dpe ni lta dgos pa med pas dben po byung ba nas yi dam gyi lha zhig gi grangs bsnyen zhig byas zhes rnam thar rje dbon mar 'byung ngo//der
grwa skor la 'byon pa'i dus su bar nas/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi gdan sa'i las chen yon tan rgya mtsho bas gtso mdzad la/ gsang phu nas byon pa'i slob dpon pa dpon slob
'di dag nged kyis?kyi skul ma byas/ bstan pa'i rgyun la bsams nas brdzangs pa yin pas khong pa la grangs chen rnams kyi steng du yang/ khong rang gi thugs bzhed ltar gyi
mdo sngags rig gnas kyis brgyan pa'i pod grangs lnga bcu la grwa skor byas mchog pa sogs phul du gang che'i bkur sti yang dag rang dgos zhes pa'i bka' shog nan tan rang gnang
nas phebs/ der paN chen rin po che nyid dgung lo nyer brgyad kyi steng du son pa shing mo phag lo'i zla ba lnga pa'i ngo dkar tsam yin gsung zhing/ sngar ngor du grwa
pa khams pa'i dger rgan zhig gis mkhan chen g.yag pas mdzad pa'i rtags rigs zhig gi phyed phul ba'i nub mnal lam na/ pu tra yin snyam pa'i a tsa ra dungvc: or: dud?long
can zhig na re/ 'di g.yag pa'i phyag dpe phyag ris ma dngos yin/ 'di'i phyed po yang khyed la gtong ngo zer ba zhig byung ba'i mnal lam de'i ched du sang gnas mjal la dga'
ldan bla brang du phebs dgongs pa'i nub/ bla brang de'i dkon gnyer gyi rmi lam du/ mkhan chen g.yag pa yin zer ba'i dge bshes bongs ring cig byung nas nga rang gi dpe
cha lta ba la yong gsung ba'i sgang la gnyid sad/ de'i sang paN chen rin po che dpon slob rnam pas phebs pas/ dkon gnyer des mdang

gi rmi lam zhus shing/ khyed rang mkhan chen g.yag pa dngos su gda' bas phyag dpe gang dgos snoms mdzod/ ces dad pa'i mchi ma phyung ste zhabs la phyag byas/ der paN chen rin
po ches phra phu ba la/ phyag dpe po ti gcig la phyag mdzub gtad nas de long gsung ba'i dbu rang nas sngar gyi rtags rigs kyi phyed kha de 'dug pas/ dpon slob der tshogs
pa kun thugs ya mtshan du gyur cing/ der mkhan chen g.yag pa'i sku'i skye bar gdan sa'i che btsun yongs kyis dgongs nas/ zhabs tog dang gsol jabya zhu ba rang gis nyin
mtshan 'da' bar gyur to//'di skabs rnam thar rdor rgyal mar/ der grwa skor dus thug cing/ phyag dpe gzigs skabs gtan nas ma byung bas/ phra phu ba'i drung gis yang yang
bskul rjes khong yid ma ches par/ nyin gcig zhogs pas bzhengs nas phyag dpe zhal bzhes gnang ba'i gzhung ma lus pa'i gzhung skyur dbu zhabs bar gsum nas phul bas/ gang la
yang bshad pa 'phros don thags thogs med par de ring bzung ba 'dra ba re gnang bas/ khyed nged tsho'i rtsar dpe lta ba skad de rdzun thabs red/ ye nas rang byung gi thams
cad mkhyen par 'dug pas ci dga' dga' mdzod/ ces zhu zhing sems rnal du 'khod ces 'byung ngo//der bzhi thog pa bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug legs pa'i 'byung gnas pa'i
drung du/ bka' 'brel 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na dkar po lha lnga'i dbang spyod pa'i rgyud las ji ltar bshad pa'i phyag bzhes kyis brgyan pa/ lha de nyid dang rjes 'brel
dpa' bo chig grub kyi rgyud/ sa skya pa rang bzhed du bkral pa'i rgyud kyi bshad lung yang 'thems pa rang zhig gsan pas/ phyis byams chen dang lam 'bras brgyud pa'i rten

rdzogs skabs/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i nang bzhugs la/ drung yig chos rgyan pa dang/ chos rje brag dmar ba kun dga' tshe 'phel drung zhal ma 'cham par/ bu ston/ sa bzang ma ti/
shar ba sogs tha dad kyi yig cha mang po dang/ jo nang mkhan po byang chub seng ge bas chos rje dpal ldan bla ma'i bka' bkod kyi dpe ris sogs mang po bsags skabs/ paN chen
rin po che'i bka' stsal la/ 'di dag nged rang lo nyer brgyad dus/ sa skyar grwa skor gyi rnam gzhag byed dus/ bdag chen gzhi thog pa'i drung du phyag khrid zhus pas 'di
ltar gsung zhes thag chod gnang ba dang/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi phyag len zin bris su bkod pa dag zhus dag byas pa ltar 'dug ces de dus rten rdzongs kyi phyag g.yog bgyid
pa po/ dol bu nam stong pa bla ma bkra shis kyi ngag las drung pa ba lung pas gsan pa'i 'phros so//de dus rgyun gyi phyag srol dbyar nyi log 'phral dus sbyor gza' skar
dge ba la grwa skor gyi mdzad pa bstan pa'i mig rkyen la phan pa stsal zhing/ sa skya rang du grags pa'i phar tshad/ 'dul mngon/ sdom rigs/ mngon pa mdzod/ tshad ma mdo/
tshad ma rnam nges/ rtsa 'jug bzhigzhi gsum/ byams chos phyi ma bzhi/ spyod 'jug/ so sor thar pa'i mdo rnams kyi steng du yum rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ theg bsdus/ dbyig
gnyen gyi sum cu pa/ nyi shu pa/ phung po lnga'i rab byed/ sa skya pa'i thugs zhen las ngor nas ched kyis bka' stsal ba'i thub pa dgongs gsal/ mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo/ sgra
nyer mkho bsdus pa/ gso ba rig pa'i bstan bcos/ sdeb sbyor me tog gi chun po/ mngon brjod tshig gter/ snyan ngag mkhas pa'i kha rgyan/ legs bshad rin po che'i gter rnams
sa skya paNDi

tas mdzad pa la ched du brjod pa'i tshul du gzhung dbu zhabs tshang ma bshad pa dang/ de'i rgyab 'grel mtshon par/ sgra mdo ka lA pa/ snyan ngag me long/ sdeb sbyor rin chen
'byung gnas/ mngon brjod a ma ra ko Sha/ klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar/ sman dpyad yan lag brgyad pa/ thon mi sambho Ta'i sum rtags/ samaRa ti dznyA na'i smra sgo/ rje
btsun rtse mo'i byis 'jug rnams dang/ sku'i phyag tshang dus 'khor dang sdom 'byung nas bstan tshul/ nang rig gi mtshon byed rgyud la 'jug pa'i sgo ste/ rgyud sde spyi rnam
dang/ chos la 'jug pa'i sgos mtha' brten nas tshogs su chos khri khar mtha' dpyad rgyas shing smin pa spyi 'gror stsal zhing/ slar gzhi thog nyid du sa skya'i che dgu
'ba' zhig gi nang chen gral dbus su kye rdor rgyud gsum/ sems 'grel skor gsum/ 'jam dpal mtshan brjod dang/ 'jam dpal zhal lung/ sgrub thabs mdo byas/ mdo sde rnam gzhag
rim pa/ spyod bsdus sgron me sogs kyi sngags gzhung/ de dag gi bshad tshom dang/ mthar rab tu gnas pa'i rgyud kyi bshad pa rgyas pa'i bar gnang zhing/ der dpal ldan sa skya'i
gnas dang/ gong ma lnga la mtshan spel ba'i mchod brjod gnang nas sgo gong du sbyar bas 'di lta bu'i snyan ngag su zhig gis bris zhes gleng ba na/ de'i phyi nyin/ de
skad smra ba nga yin sogs nga brgyad ma sbyar byang du bkod do//phyags phyi tshal pa rin rgyal phra phu ba sangs rgyas bzang po la sogs pa rnams kyis spyi 'gro'i grwa skor
yang dag dang/ khyad par rigs pa'i sgo nas grags pas sa stengs ma lus pa khyab par byas so//tshul 'di dag rnam thar gsum gar du mi 'byung mod kyang/ de'i dus kyi gzhung
las par gyur pa sa skya pa las chen yon tan

rgya mtsho ba dngos las/ gting skyes rab 'byams pa sde bdun dbang phyug rgyal mtshan pas gsan pa'i ngag rgyun 'phel ba las rnyed pa dag go//der 'dus pa'i mkhas rmongs nas byis
pa'i bar rang dbang ma mchis pa'i dad pa'i spu long g.yos shing/ rgyang ring po nas kyang sku'i rgyal mtshan mthong ba'i mod la phyag 'tshal ba dang/ ngag nas ched du
brjod pa'i nga ros skyabs su mchi/ zhes thal mo sbyor bar byed pa'i mos dge'i sa bon rgya cher bskrun nas/ slar e waM chos ldan bla ma'i bzhugs gnas ngor dgon gsar du phebs
shing/ de rjes rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po dges pa mchog tu 'khrungs te bzhugs gdan gyi bkur sti sogs kyang blo 'das kyi dbu 'don stsal bas/ phyis ngor tshor rgyal
tshab kun dbang pa'i dus phebs skabs kan tsa'i stengs su phebs shing/ rje bla mas stsal ba'i gdan khur yin no gsung/ sngar gyi bzhugs gdan mtho la spus gtsang ba'i bkur
sti ma nyams par mdzad pa'i tshul/ ngor zur 'chang ba slob dpon bsod nams sangs rgyas pa'i dbon po'i kha sgo nas thos so//der rje rdo rje 'chang chen gyis grwa skor gyi
legs ja'i stengs su/ sngon sa skya paNDi ta la kha che paN chen gyis gnang ba yin gsung ba'i ston pa'i rgya sku li ma/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa rin po che'i snam sbyar re nyid
kyi sku la rgyun bzhes lo nyi shu rtsa lnga gnang/ de'i ring gi rab gnas dbang bskur bsnyen rdzogs sogs kyi byin rlabs can/ hor gos lu haM sku dreg dang bcas pa tshul khrims
kyi dris phyogs bcur khyab pa de dang/ dbus gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas pas phul ba'i gsol lhung rnams stsal zhing/ 'di dag byams pa'i nang bzhugs nyid la yod nges
dkar chag gis mtshon par nus la/ gzhan rje nyid lta zhog phyag g.yog gi grwa skor gnang ba'i tshal pa rin rgyal

phra phu sangs rgyas bzang po ba sogs la'ang/ gos lu haM srab mo'i chos gos sogs gnang sbyin yang dag gi bka' drin mdzad/ phyis de dus bzhugs gral la bdag chen chu mig pa'i
drung dang/ shar pa bdag chen ye shes dbang phyug par grags pa'i sku na gzhon nu rdo rje 'chang chen pos bkur sti sa skya bdag chen pa las kyang che che tsam gnang ba zhig
gral gyi dbu la bzhugs 'dug cing/ phyis rdo rje 'chang zhing brjes nas lo skor gcig song ba'i phyi lo/ rang res rje don yod dpal ba mjal ba la rkang gtad yongs dus/ chu
mig tshor chos zhu ba la yun ring bsdad skabs/ bdag chen rin po ches sbon gyi de'i skyor zlos gnang/ nged kyis rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs drung du mi lo gsum cu
so bgrangs gcig 'bral med bsten kyang/ khyed la dges dges de lta bu dang/ khyed rnams la yang de dus gnang ba'i gnang sbyin dpe bral de 'dra su la yang gnang ba mi dran
pa lags shes thugs ha las las mdzad nas gsung zhes/ rdo ring rin po che dngos las thos so//der rje rdo rje 'chang gis bde mchog/ rnal 'byor ma'i skor gyi dbang byin rlabs/
chos skyong sogs dbang khang du chig brgyud du gnang nas/ 'di dag la thugs dam gyi snying po mdzos cig ces dang/ sa skya paNDi tas bsgyur ba'i rdo rje snying po rgyan/
gsang ba nor bu sogs rgyud gsum dang/ lhag par gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid dang/ kha che paN chen dang sa paN gnyis kyis lo paN gnang ba'i/ slob dpon sgra gcan 'dzin dpal
bshes gnyen kyis mdzad pa'i gsang 'dus kyi dkyil chog ras bris la brten pa zung 'jug gsal bar grags pa de'i lung yang stsal nas/ gsang 'dus 'di la rang gzhan shan 'byed
pa'i bshad pa dang/ yi ge yang dag rtsom zhes kyang bka' bsgo ba thugs

la bzhag/ phyis gser mdog can thebs rjes/ gsang 'dus rnam bshad rnam par thar pa'i sgo brgya pa'i thugs rtsom dang/ par yang bsgrubs pas/ ngor gyi rdo rje 'chang gi gzims mal
sku 'dra'i drung du 'bul mi gnang/ de dus ngor gdan sar chos rje 'dren mchog bzhugs pa'i dus yin pas/ dpe'i phyi 'dril kha thags dkar po dri ma med pa zhig la phyag rtags
'byar ba de'i rgya yang ma nyams par chos rje rin po che nyid kyi phyag gis rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku 'dra'i phyag chos 'chad gnang ba'i bar du phul nas/ bdag
lo bcu gsum pa la ngor du phyin dus kyang mig gis rig cing/ chos rje lha mchog pa'i sku ring la yang de kar yod kyang/ ding sang ni dgag sgrub byed pa'i dpe lta la song zer
gar yang ma dmigs lags so//de rjes rdo rje 'chang gi bka' lung la/ chos bdag po'i dper 'dug cing/ rang re'i mig gis mi chod par 'dug pas/ bdag po chu mig pa'i drung du
sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung zhu dang/ chos skyong gi skor rnams zhus mdzod/ rang res dngos kyi bkri thabs bgyid gsung nas/ de'i lo'i dbyar smad chu mig tu sa skya pa chen
po'i bka' 'bum dang/ chos skyong lcam dral gyi rjes gnang sgrub skor rdzogs par byung rjes ston chag la yang ngor du phyin/ bsnyen rdzogs pa mang po'i las slob dgyis gsung
ba bzhin bsgrubs/ bka' chos slar yang rtsa dbu ma'i khrid cig byung zhing/ gzhan yang lam zab phyi nang dang byas pa'i 'dod chos 'ga' re thob/ der zhabs la phyag bgyis/
rang re mtshan nyid pa skam po mig tu sgog skya bcug na min pa mchi ma mi 'chor rigs yin kyang/ bla ma de'i mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan khyad par can la dang ba'i
dad pa snying khong nas skyes pa'i mthus mig chu 'dzag pa'i rgyun mi chod bzhin du 'ongs zhes paN chen dngos las rje btsun

kun dga' mchog grub kyis gsan pa'i gsung sgros so//der zha lu'i rten mjal la bsnyags nas lcags brgyud yongs/ de dus zha lu mkhan por gtsang ston chos grub dpal bzang par grags
pa de tsho bzhugs kyi 'dug kyang/ rang re bla mas dregs pa'i mjal mjal kyang ma byas zha lu ri phug na sgra pa chen po gnas brtan legs rgyal ba tsho bzhugs 'dug pas rang
re la gzhi len gzab rgyas stsal/ sngar sa skyar brtsams pa'i dpal ldan sa skya'i gnas dang gang zag la sgra las drangs pa'i bstod pa ngag gi dbang po'i dga' ston de phyag
tu byung 'dug pas thugs la byang bar bzhugs 'dug/ de la 'di'i nang na gau sgra don dgu la 'dugvc: or: 'jug?pa'i ba lang la glang chen dkar pos bteg pa'i khri steng du
zer ba 'di la glang po'i skad dod hasti yin dus/ gau ba lang la 'grig/ don du yang 'jam dbyangs kyi rigs rnams seng khri 'ba' zhig rang bshad pas/ glang por mi yong bas
nged la the tshom bag tsam byung/ gzhan 'di 'dra sus shes gsung/ der de ma thag sngar dpyad pa ma zhugs na'ang/ rig gnas la sbyangs pa'i mthar byon pa'i bka' lung ji lta

rab tu byed pa bcu gnyis pa'o// //Chapter 13: ngo mtshar gyi dum bu 'ga' zhigder gsang phu'i dbyar dgun gyi dus chos la bya dus btab pa ltar g.yo ba med ngos lcags pho
'brug vc: 1460/ lcags mo sbrul vc: 1461/ chu pho rta vc: 1462/ chu mo luglugs vc: 1463/ shing pho spre'u vc: 1464ste de nyid kyi dgung lo so bdun du son pa'i bar gyi lo

pa//bkra shis shing rtas drangs pa'i rgyu skar mgon//smon lam dag pa'i mkha' dbyings dbus der shar//mkhyen yang bya lam khyon der shes bya'i yul//ma lus thogs med yongs
su gsal ba na//kun khyab grags pa'i rnga chen phyogs bcu'i 'gron//ma bos ngang gis

blta phyir 'ongs pa snyam//'jig rten mes pos ma byas srid 'di na//gang yang mi mngon sgrog tshe 'di lta'i tshul//rgyal ba mchog gi mdzad pa sgyu ma'i 'phrul//ngo mtshar 'di
'dra tshangs pa'i yul las 'das//tshogs gnyis shing rta'i 'khor los nyer drangs pas//yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag po slob ma'i tshogs//sangs rgyas sras bcas rgyal po'i khab
tu bzhin//ya mtshan 'di ni snyigs ma'i dus las brgal//lhar bcas 'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing gyur pa//'dul ba mdo sde mngon pa 'dzin pa'i rje//chos smra'i skye bo mchog khyed
rnyed bkur gyis//rab bsngags khri la khengs pa med par bzhugs//gang gi rjes slob dgra bcom 'phags pa'i 'khor//zhi zhing rab zhi ngur smrig gos can gyi//tshul gnas mang
thos mthar son spong ba pas//mnga' ris yul ljongs dge ba'i phan bde stsal//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib
mo rnam par 'byed pa las mnga' ris kyi yul 'khor du chos sgra sgrags pa'i skabs las rjes su bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa bco lnga pa'o// //Chapter 16: yid dam gyis rjes su
gzung ba dang mngon par mkhyen pa'i gnasder sdom gsum gyi dri ba thog ma rang de/ glo bo'i lung lag nyi phug dgon pa na mkhan po seng ge bzang por grags pa bzod pa skya
gshog pa'i dngos slob cig bzhugs pa de la phul bas/ tshig sbyor sogs po tol che ba'i phal nyams can zhig byung bas cung zhig thugs mdzangs shing/ rang res bstan pa'i byi
dor la bsams/ lhag bsam rnam dag gis yin kyang/ der mi mtshon pa'i brjod gleng can gyi ku co'i rgyur 'gro ba zhig yong ba 'dra gsung/ thugs dben mdzad pa'i tshul yang bstan
zhing/ de mtshams rwa ston yon tan dpal bzang pos/sa paN gsung gi nyi ma'i 'od//mi shes sprinsprin sprin

gyis bsgrib pa'i cha//legs byas dri ba'i rlung gzhon gyis//bstan bcos 'od ris gsal bar mdzad//ces sogs ched du brjod pa'i snyan mgag dang rjes 'brel gyi dris lan zhig phul
bas/ snga ma'i tshig sgra de khegs snang ngo gsung dges pa 'khrungs shing/ yang chos zom lba ba/ mtshan dngos shes rab seng ger grags pa des kyang dris lan zhig phul bas/
de'i don bsdu phyis gser thur du 'dri dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan/ ma dris na bstan bcos chud za ba/ dris lan dngos dang gsum gyi/ bar pa'i cha de khol por phyung ba lta bu'i
lan 'debs/ slar dri ba gnad la 'bebs 'dra'i bstan bcos shig spyan lam du thogs pas/ der paN chen rin po che yang dges pa mchog tu 'khrungs te mnga' ris na mdo sngags kyi
tshul la sbyangs pa mthar phyin pa'i mkhas pa 'di 'dra yang snang/ ngo mtshar zhes dang/ shes rab seng ger ming btags pa don mthun du 'dug go// zhes kyang yang yang bka'
stsol bar mdzad ces/ bdag gi bla ma mkhas pa'i dbang po dpal ldan tshul khrims pa'i gsung las thos so//de rjes gzhi byes kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen phra rags kun gyi grwa skor
gnang mtshams/ shar nas byon pa'i dpon slob yongs la 'bul ba'i rnam gzhag/ tsan dan jo bos gtso byas pa'i zangs/ gser/ spos shel/ byi ru mu tig/ ras sngon dmar/ bzang
drug sogs stod zong spus dag gi 'bul ba dpag med phul/ sgal ma rta nyi shu tsam dge 'dun spyi 'gror phul zhing/ phyis 'di skabs kyi 'phros glang thang spyan snga grub rgyal
bas/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pa'i drung tshor zhus pa'i brjod gleng thos pa la/ de dus grwa pa snyoms chung shos la yang lo gsum re'i rgyags mthud yong nges byung
zhing/ de las kyang dpon slob sum brgya lo gsum gyi ring dbyar dgun so so'i

gos mal thogs med de rang ha las pa byung/ paN chen rin po che la 'bul ba'i rnam gzhag blo las 'das pa 'dug kyang de'i nang nas tsan dan dkar dmar mi'i rgyab khur theg tshad
kyi sdong po gnyis dang/ byi ru'i rgyal mo lag pa yal ga sum cu so bdun la dbangs rtse khur longs pa zhig snang ba de kun yang ngo mtshar che bar 'dug zhu zhes stag lung
du thos so//der g.yas ru byang nas chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang pas dus 'khor sman dpyad skor la dri ba du mar gnang ba'i lan 'bul ba dang/ da nged kyang lo brgyad
bcu gya gnyis stengs su slebs/ nyi ma gangs thog tu 'khyol ba yin pas phyis mjal ba'i spros pa med/ da res cis kyang mjal ba'i thugs tsham dor ngos/ lam byang phyogs la
'byon dgos gsung nas phebs lam byang la gnang zhing/ der chos rgyal bkra shis mgon pas mar lam paN chen rin po che la/ nang ras par ma khro mo legs pos byas phyi so ba 'ga'
ji dkar pos byas pa'i gur/ yol gcod kyi phugs su gzim chung dang bde spyod nyis sbrag/ mdor yol ba phyogs gang gsal de la g.yab kha phyogs der bstan/ yol skor gnang dus
gzims khang ka bzhi yangs pa tsam gyi khyon ka ba sogs cher mi dgos pa'i 'phrul rgya gar bzo khyad 'don zhig phul bas/ mthong ba kun blo 'das kyi ya mtshan du byed cing/
phyis gser mdog can gyi gos sku g.yed can bsgrub nas rab gnas gnang dus yo ya mtshan du sgrog cing/ slob dpon mya ram pa'i zhal nas/ sngon glo bo nas phul ba'i ras gur
khyad 'don de kun khyed tshosvc: or: chos?ma mthong ba yin yod/ nga la ni gos sku bkram pa de la thang ka chen po zhig gi mthong las med gsungs pas der tshogs kun bzhad cha
byung zhing/ der paN chen rin po che'i zhal nas/ sngon gyi de la

yang gur lha khang ma zer ba yin gsung/ mtshar po rang cig yod ces sprul sku sman thang pas bshad do//der chos rgyal bkra shis mgon yab sras rnams kyis nyin lam gsum gyi bar
du skyel ma mdzad/ mthar gser gyi maNDal phul/ zhabs spyi bor blangs/ gdung ba'i spyan chab g.yo zhing smon lam dpag med btab nas/ slar glo bo nang du phebs/ paN chen rin
po che dpon slob kun kyang mar lam shul bde bar byang ngam rings su phebs/ der dbyar chos kyi sgang du snang bas rigs pa'i bro gar so sor bsgyur zhing/ mkhan chen spo
ra ba 'jigs med grags pa bzhugs pas/ spyan 'dren zhus/ phan tshun phyag rkyong ba gang bder gnang zhing/ zhabs tog bsnyen bkur yang dag pas phebs lam gyi dub pa bsal/ der
sdom rigs kyi dri ba las brtsams pa'i 'bel gtam yang sgo du ma nas gnang ngo//de mtshams lhun sdings su chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang dang mjal nas/ chos kyi 'bel gtam
mang du mdzad pas thugs lhag par rangs te/ drung chen po ba rang gis bla ma'i gtso bor bkur ba'i chos rje rong ston shes bya kun rig pa dang/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang
po ba gnyis ka dang nged 'phrad cing/ chos kyi dri mal mtha' yas pa byed myong na'ang/ 'di 'dra'i phyogs tsam yang med/ rang re'i bsam pa la rje thams cad mkhyen pa phyogs
las rnam rgyal ba zhing brjes phyin/ bod yul 'dir bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi mig rkyen khur ba'i smra ba po cig mi srid snyam pa'i yid khong du bsdus yod kyang/ da sems
sos shes dges pa'i bka' lung dpag med stsal/ der paN chen nyid kyis kyang dus 'khor gyi bka' 'phrang ma bde ba kun/ ja gral du gleng slong gi zhu mal kho nas sgrog khrol
te/ phyis mtshan nas smos dus rigs ldan padma dkar po zhes nye tsher

gsung zhing/ der dus kyi 'khor lo sdom pa chen po'i dbang bskur yang gsan/ de nas dpon slob rnams shar phyogs su phebs dus/ byang pa la rgyal khrims mig rkyen srung mi med
pas mnga' ris kyi rdzas stobs che ba mig tu ma tshud par/ chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang pa bzhugs nas tsha lam tsam gyi sar/ nar khu g.yung drung zer ba'i sdig can des
chom po byas/ dngos po gong khal 'ga' re phrogs lhag par drung chen sangs rgyas seng ge la/ brla la mdung rtse dam pa zhig phog nas rmas so//der de'i nyin rang chos rgyal
rnam rgyal grags pas gsan nas/ de'i srod la thugs dam gtor ma zur drug pa 'phangs pas bstan gshigs de'i khang pa'i stengs du me sgra dang bcas babs/ der dngos po phren
tshegs de rnams thugs kyis btang/ lam srangs nas 'byon 'dod la/ byang nas zhu nan byas re shig 'jad mthong smon du bzhugs shing/ de'i ring rgyud 'bum gzigs rtog dang/ grangs
chen bco brgyad la sngar rgol du zhal bzhes kyi dam bca' bkod pa'i grub mtha' bsdus pa de yang mdzad/ der chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags pa nyid kyis che thang du bkas
bcad nas/ sku rgyal blo 'das dang/ drung chen sangs rgyas seng ge la yang rgyal ka chen po'i yus 'dogs mdzad/ de rjes ston ser gser mdog can du phebs/ rje don yod dpal ba
dang yab sras zhal mjal gnang mtshams/ de lo dbyar de dbyar med song ba'i gsob byed dgos gsung/ tshogs pa'i mkhan chen blo gros bstan pas zhus pa'i ngor/ mdo rtsa'i dka'
'grel nyi ma'i shing rta'i thugs rtsom sku mtshams se ba'i ngang nas gnang zhing/ 'dul ba nyid sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i rtsa bar dgongs pa'i gces spras gyis las brgya'i
TI ka ba dan dkar po'i rnga dbyangs

bslab bya chen mo sogs sngon med kyi legs bshad dag cig kyang rim gyis yi ger 'khod par mdzad do//der lo gsar shar ba'i me pho spre'u vc: 1476dgung lo zhe dgur phebs pa'i dus/
thog mar ngor dgon gsar bla ma'i gdan sar mang ja 'gyed bcas zhu ba la phebs pas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug pa'i drung gis sngar ltar dpe ma mchis pa'i bka' drin
bskyangs shing/ der zla phyed tsam gyi ring la gsang 'dus 'jam rdor sa skya pa'i thugs dam gyi mthil/ bla ma gnyan lo tsa ba'i lugs kyi dbang bskur rdul tshon ma dang/
de dang rjes 'brel gsang 'dus spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang/ rgya gzhung tha dad kyi lung/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i bskyed rdzogs khyad par ba dag gsan/ der rgyal tshab kun dbang
pas khyed dbus la mi 'byon pa'i rten 'brel yod do gsung/ bcom ldan 'das mi bskyod pa'i rgya nag gi sku rtse khru gang pa gcig gi gnang sbyin yang stsal/ de mtshams chu mig
tu che sa bdag chen blo gros dbang phyug pa'i drung du phebs pas/ khyed mnga' ris su bzhugs ring thugs dam rtogs pa khyad pa can zhig 'khrungs yod par snang/ sngar nged
rang rus gog 'di ches pas rtog pa ma chud/ da ni khyed kyis phyag byas dus dpral ba tsha zhum zhum byas yong gi snang zhes che bstod dang/ bzhugs sa yang gzims chung gcig
la yol gcod mdzad nas gnang zhing/ tho rangs bdag chen drung gsung phra mos/rdo rje 'chang chen rdo rje rnal 'byor ma//grub chen nA ro pa dang pham mtheng pa//shes rab
brtsegs dang mal gyo sa skya pa//rje btsun sku mched rnams la gsol ba 'debs//kho de tsho longs ja skol/ drung chen po ba'i drung 'o brgyal gsung ba zhig yod ces/ paN chen
rin po ches gsungs pa'i gsung sgros mnga' ris su skyor mi mang po byung ngo//der da gtsang rang

du bzhugs la sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rgyun la phan pa'i 'chad nyan rang gnang dgos/ da lo thog mar chos gzhis 'di dag bskul zhing/ nged shi mtshams shi rjes gang yod mdzod
la/ chu mig stong skor 'di rnams khyed kyis 'chad nyan dang/ gser mdog can gyi thes mdzod// khyed thugs mi dog par nged rang ma shi gong nas yi ge thel 'byar byed gsung ba'i
bka' lung nan chen gnang zhing/ de'i lo rje mus chen dang/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs sher rgyam ba'i sku bstod thub bstan gser khang ma dang/ mtha' yas ma gnyis brtsams 'phral
re 'dug pa'i lung yang stsal nas/ slar yang gser mdog can du 'ongs/ de nas dbus phyogs su/ rgya ma mkhar rtse bas glo bo rang du 'bod mi byung ba dang/ khyad par du
spyang lung rin po che dgung lo brgyad dang lnga bzhes pa de'i zhal zhig mthong 'dod rang gis cis kyang dbus phyogs la 'gro rtsis rang gis zhed che ba byas kyang/ gzhis
ka nas dang/ dpon drung g.yung ba sogs kyis kyang nga dgon pa gsar pa'i 'gram bting tsam la ma bzhugs na rjes dod pa'i tshad gtan nas mi srid pas zer/ nan bskyed byung/ der
na ning yang dbyar med du song bas yid skrag/ da lo dbyar khas len byas nas/ dgag dbye grol dang bstun 'gro rtsis rang la chos sdings nas rin po che pa'i drung zla ba
bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga la zhing brjes pa'i tshul 'bul mi byung bas/ thugs khral mtha' med gnang zhing/ gdung rten gyi rgyur zangs ser mang du stsal/ da ste gnyis med seng
ge la rgyu mtshan med pas grwa tshang gi mings bzhag 'di'i so chis la bsdad pa drag snang gsung nas/ lo bzhi'i bar gtsang phyogs rang du zhabs brtan par bzhugs shing/
dgung lo zhe dgu pa'i steng de nyid du/ rgya rgan nang pas do dam mdzad/ span mi dmangs kyis ka ba

sum cu so drug gi sa'i kun ra rnying pa 'di bsgrubs shing/ 'di nyid kyi gtsang khang na bzhugs pa'i byams mgon don yod dpal ba'i sku 'dra sku tshad ma 'di rten bzhengs kyi
thog mar mdzad cing/ 'di nyid sku dngos ji lta pa'i 'dra len gyis/ dbu'i gtsug tor gsal por 'phags pa yang bcos yod pas/ rab gnas la rje don yod dpal ba rang gdan 'dren zhus
pas/ gzigs mo yang yang mdzad nas bzhed cing/ der dbu zhwa zhwa ser cig zhus yod pa bsal bas/ dbu'i gtsug tor gzigs pas/ phyag gis nem mnan nas 'an bu la 'di 'dra mi
bdog gsungs pas rjes med du gyur ces de dus dngos su gzigs pa'i mnga' ris pa rnams kyis gsungs pas mnga' ris na grags tshod shin tu che zhing/ bka' las kyang 'di la rab gnas
zhal dro rang zhig byung bas/ phyis kyi rten thams cad la bar chad med pa'i rten 'brel rabvc: or: rang?'grig la song zhes gsung/ zhes thos shing/ da lta yang dge ba'i
ltas la dbu zhwa rgyab/ mi dge ba la mdun ngos bskyur yong zhing/ rtog pa bcug na zhal gyi gzi mdangs dang/ zhal ngo nag mi nag rang gis legs nyes 'byed par snang ngo//der
me mo bya'i lo vc: 1477dgung lo lnga bcu'i steng du dpyid chos la gzhis ka nas sbyin bdag gnang/ 'brong sgang nas zhabs tog bsgrubs te sreg shing du mdzad pas/ sngar bzhin
sa skya paN chen gyi chos khri nyid kyi steng nas dpyid chos mdzad/ der rjes dbyar zhal bzhes 'du khang rnying pa nyid du gnang zhing/ dus tshigs kyi mdo 'don pa sogs
la thugs brtson che ba'i khur bzhes mdzad pas/ drung nas chos kyi bzang po bas/ rang re'i rje'i drung chen po ba kun kyang/ dge ldan pa la skrus pa'i dbyar gnas 'dis tha
na grwa pa'i chos ka 'tshol ba tshun la zhag bdun las 'gro sa med pa 'di

gu rang dog ces/ de gong sa skya pa la sngagsbsngags pa lta zhog/ mtshan nyid pa rang la yang 'dul ba'i mig rkyen ci yang ma dmigs pa 'dis mtshon to//gzhan yang gnas brtan
tshul blo ba la/ phyis paN chen rin po ches zhal kur gnang dus/ sngon rje don yod dpal ba'i grwa pa rnams rgyal btsugs nas/ khyi shig bsad pa la sdom pa 'chor mi 'chor de
la/ da gnas brtan nas ci gsung/ gsungs pas/ los 'chor lags/ 'dul ba na srog gcod pa dang zhes gsungs shing khyi shig la srog yod pa la 'os ci yod/ rgyun du zhu ba ltar 'chad
nyan rgyugs len las/ grub mtha'i nges gzung smos ci/ tha snyad gang la'ang brdar ma thogs pa zhig las med/ phyis paN chen rin po che'i sku tshe'i stod la/ mnga' ris
pa'i slob gnyer ba 'dra yar slebs dus thun mong zin thun bskyar bas/ rje don yod dpal ba'i grwa rgan yon tan che ba rang du byas pa gcig na re/ khyed kun gyis rig pa sgrims
shig/ ngas byams mgon don yod dpal bzang po'i drung du/ mi lo chen po nyi shu rtsa gcig bsdad de/ dpal ldan chos kyi grags pa'i tshad ma sde bdun bya ba las ming ma thos/
mngon pa sde bdun dang kha 'chal de 'dra mis tshor ro zer byung ba la/blo gsar pa de kun gyi sagyis? //ye shes la 'jug ka tya bus//rab tu byed pa dbyig bshes kyi//rnam
shes tshogs ni lha skyid kyis//chos kyi phung po shA ri'i bus//gdags pa'i bstan bcos mo'u 'gal bus//'gro ba'i rnam grangs gsus po ches//khams kyi tshogs ni gang pos bsdus//shes
mdzad pa po'i dgra bcom pa bdun dang bcas pa'i ming gsal bar brjod pas/ khong bgres po de na re/ 'dug 'dug ngo mtshar che'o zer ba yang byung zhes gtam yod do//sa
pho khyi lo vc: 1478dgung lo lnga bcu nga gcig stengs su/ sngar

gsang phur bdud sde bcom pa'i ltas khyad par ba'i mtshan ma bstan pa'i dbu ma'i stong thun che chung gnyis dang/ phar phyin gyi spyi don chen mo'i brtsams chos kyi dbu btsugs
te/ rim gyis mthar phyin par mdzad la/ sngar mnga' ris su dgung lo zhe gcig dus/ gnas gsum gsal byed/ kun mkhyen rong po'i rnam thar/ sdom gsum gyi dri ba sogs kyi yig
mkhan kong ston mgon po rgyal mtshan yin zhing/ phyis dgung lo don bdun bar gyi rtsom yig drung nas lo tsa ba chos rgyal mtshan pas gnang/ khong rgya gar la gshegs phyin/
bde mchog rnam bshad/ byams chos lam rim sogs sku tshe mthar phyin gyi gsung rtsom dag gi yi ge pa ni da lta'i a zhang bsod lhun pa nyid yin la/ drung yig chos rgyan pa
yang glo bo'i sde pa bkra shis mgon pas spyan lam du thogs pa rang ma byung bas/ mnga' ris gung thang tshor phebs/ mngon dga' chos sder mkhas btsun dpal ldan dar gyi drung
du sgra'i sa ris/ snyan ngag/ sdeb sbyor/ rgya yig rnam grangs du ma'i bslab sbyangs yang dag gnang rjes/ khong pas khyod blo gsal bar 'dug pas bstan pa la phan pa srid/
mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer la bkra shis lhun por byon gsung ba ltar byon nas phar phyin gyi lung 'bring tsam mdzad skabs/ mnga' ris glo bo'i grwa pa brag dkar chos rje
yon tan bzang po dang/ drung btsun shes rab dpal 'byor bas blo brkus nas sa skya par zhal bsgyur te/ paN chen rin po che'i zhabs drung tshor phebs/ drung nas shangs pa la
phar tshad dbu gsum gyi gtong chos zhus nas/ thogthoka mar thugs gnyer rang lo sbrel mdzad rjes// rim gyis rig gnas kyi sku yon la dpagsvc: or: dbags?nas/ paN chen rin
po che'i spyan lam thogs te rtsom yig gi mthil ma gnang ba'i bka' 'bum phal cher

du/ yi ge pa ni blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan no zhes 'byung bas so//lo tsa ba 'dis kyang tshad ma'i brgyud 'debs kha che paN chen gyi gong ma/ wa gIndra paNDi ta ste paN
chen ngag dbang zer ba la/ wa bu paN chen dang/ paNDi ta chos kyi nyin byed kyis rgya gar gyi lam nas zhu yig phul ba'i rgya skad la/ dharma dI pa ka ra zhes bod skad chos
kyi nyin byed la chos kyi snang byed du byas pa/ 'jam dbyangs dkar po'i sa bon/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas a las byung/ zhes a thung yin pa la 'brug gsum gyi zlas phye ba'i
AH yig tu bris pa sogs dpyad rgyu cung zad cig 'dug kyang/ sngon ni sus kyang gleng brjod ma mdzad snang ngo//de'i dpyid chos la nyug rgyal khang du phebs shing/ der mnga'
ris glo bo nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug pa'i drung zhing brjes pa'i mang ja zhu mi sleb pas/ lnga mchod pa sogs sngar glo bor bka' chos zhus pa'i grwa rigs/
bdag gi bla ma rje btsun kun dga' mchog grub/ paN chen byams pa gling pa dpal ldan tshul khrims pa sku mched/ brag dkar chos rje yon tan bzang po ba/ dbu mdzad kun rgyal
ba sogs drag rigs re res thos mchod la mang ja re zhus zhing/ der paN chen rin po che dang/ dgon pa shar na rje don yod dpal ba bzhugs pa'i yab sras gnyis ka'i drung du
bsngo rten so so dang bcas pa zla phyed tsam bsgrubs rjes/ paN chen rin po che'i gsung gis/ nged kyis thos mchod la/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi bka' 'bum gyi lung zhig sgrog gsung/
nyug pa'i phyag dpe'i steng nas pod bzhi ma'i lung zhag re la po ti phyed phyed zhag brgyad la rdzogs par gnang zhing/ sngar smros pa'i mnga' ris pa'i che btsun de
rnams kun gyis gsan no//dbyar zhal bzhes gser mdog can du mdzad cing/ 'di'i lo mngon pa kun las btus kyi dka' 'grel gyi thugs rtsom yang gnang/ de'i grub mtha' bsdus pa dang/
rab byed gsum gyi TI ka yang phyis mdzad do//de ltar gtsang phyogs su lug spre bya khyi vc: 1475-78ste lo ngo bzhi gdan chags/ gtsang phyogs kyi phrin las kyi rmangs
gzhi things nas/ slar glang thang nas spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan pa'i chos 'khor rtse'i grwa sdud byas pa'i/ grwa pa 'di phyogs kyi drag bsdus rang 'di dag rab byung
gnang ba'i ched du de nas zhabs ma bskyod na/ nged rnam pa che phra kun gyi bsam pa gtan mi gang ba yod pas shes nan zhus rang gnang ba'i dbang las/ dbus phyogs su chibs
kha bsgyur ba gnang skad do//'di skabs rnam thar rje dbon mar/ gser 'phyang me mo bya lo vc: 1477'phebs gsung ba ni thugs rtog ma chug pa yin te/ de ltar na lo bzhi gtsang
du bzhugs shes gong du bris pa la lo gcig mi tshang bas so//de nas sa pho khyi lo vc: 1478smin drug gi zla ba ngo dkar tsam la gtsang phyogs nas zhabs zung gi 'khor
lo bskyod bde bar bskul te/ rin spungs nas dpon slob thams cad la gsol phogs/ lam chas rgya cher btab nas/ sde snod 'dzin pa brgya phrag lnga lhag tsam gyis mdun nas bdar
bzhin du/ ngur smrig gi jo mo sgrol ma'i drung du snyan dar/ dkar me/ gser chab zhus/ dpon slob yongs kyis lhan cig gsol btab gnang nas/ rim gyis dpal bde dang/ gong dkar/
lum pa rnams kyi zhag phog dang bstun pa'i zhabs tog bsgrub pa'i ngang

nas/ drang srong srin po ri'i bde mchog mjal ba la phebs shing/ de'i nub paN chen rin po che'i zhal snga nas/ bde mchog lha khang nyid du gzims pas/ srod kyi cha la bde mchog
lha dpa' bo gcig pa de nyid zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa'i skur gzigs shing/ de'i glang lpags nam mkha' la gdugs bskor ba ltar gzigs nas/ paN chen

nyid kyang thugs dam zil che ba'i ngang nas/ re zhig phyag gi bzhugs stangs gzigs snang ltar la yun ring du bzhugs pa drung chen sangs rgyas seng ge bas mthong la/ rgyu mtshan
gtan tshigs dang 'brel ba ni/ drung yig chos rgyan pas dgongs te drung btsun shes rab dpal 'byor ba la gsungs pa las bdag gis thos shing/ 'di thad rnam thar gsum ka na
mthun par srin po rir bde mchog gi gzigs snang byung zhes tha dad na bkod yod do//de nas rim gyis 'phrang por phebs/ zla gcig gi gsol phogs phul ring chos ra rigs lung
smar ba gnang/ de mtshams shel grong nas zla phyed phogs shig phul ba la lam chas su mdzad nas/ chos 'khor lha sa'i jo bo rin po che la gser chab 'bul ba sogs dang/ dpon
slob yongs kyis smon lam rgya cher gnang rjes/ grwa pa bying rnams gzhung lam bsrangs rgya ma khri khang du rdzong ba mdzad/ paN chen rin po che dpon slob drag bsdus rang
zhig spyang lung du phebs/ spyang lung rin po che'i thugs ljags spyan gsum byon pa mjal ba gnang zhing/ lhag par sngar spyang lung rin po che zhal bzhugs dus phyag nas 'byar
ba'i sku 'dra sku tshad ma bla ma dngos byon te steng gi g.yabs lho bstan na yod pa'i drung du phebs nas mjal ba'i mod la/ sku 'dra rin po che de'i spyan gnyis las 'od
zer sna snga nyi ma'i mtha'i 'od 'phreng lta bu 'phro ba der 'dus yongs kyis mthong zhing/ de dus drin can spyang lung pa gzhon nu chos grub pa'i zhal snga nas dgung lo
bco lnga bzhes pa zhig yod gsung zhing/ paN chen rin po che dang zhal mjal ba'i sngon ma rang de yin na'ang de'i lo bka' 'brel ni ma thob/ phyag dbang tsam ka yin zhes
dngos su gsung ngo// phyag dbang tsam ka yin zhes dngos su gsung ngo//sbyangs gnas phra ba'i yon tan dpag dka'i dngos//cher rlom rgyang mig spyod

pas mthong min kyang//shin tu zab mo'i rnam dpyod gsal ldan pa//gting mtha' med pa'i blo gros legs byas shes//brtsang dris brtags pas mkhas pa phal gyi gting//yongs su mi rtogs
gangs can ljongs 'dir su//gang nas smras kyang de nyid la sbyangs tshul//blo gros mi zad spobs pa brtsegs par grags//dus 'khor rin chen gzhal med khang bzangs rtser//blo
chung phal gyis bgrod pa'i spobs med la//rigs ldan ye shes gzigs pa'i yul 'dzin khyod//dka' ba med par tshul der byang chub gyur//thos tsam mkhyen pa'i rang bzhin khyed
la yang//ma thos sgrib byed snyems byed 'di mtshar to//yud kyis nyer dgongs the tshom phra ba'i cha//khyed thugs la 'jug gzhan ngor ston min nam//bzod pa'i rang mtshan
bzod 'bras yid 'phrog sku//drang po'i rang babs drang por stsol ba'i gsung//gdod nas rab zhi gdod nas dag pa'i thugs//yon tan rgyan ldan yon tan 'od ltar 'khums//bstan
dang 'gro ba'i don byed gang gi thugs//yongs su bskul bas 'bad med chos ston gsung//dad pa'i shing rta 'dren byed yid 'phrog sku//thugs gsung sku yi dkyil 'khor lta na sdug//yi
dam yongs grub gzigs pa'i dpal gang gis//gzhan dbang mdzes pa'i gar bsgyur ngo mtshar gnas//kun brtags gdul bya'i ngor yang brtse ba can//ye shes rab bkra'i spyan
lnga lhun gyis grub//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ yid dam gyis rjes su gzung ba dang
mngon par mkhyen pa'i gnas las bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa bcu drug pa'o//Chapter 17: mkhas pa'i mdzad pa'i mig 'phrulder rgya ma'i gtsug lag khang der gzhi

byes kyi tshogs pa ma lus pa la zla phyogs bzang ba zhig gi bsnyen bkur phul nas/ chos ra rigs lung sogs lhag par smar bar gnang zhing/ der sku 'chag pa la sngon rgya ma sangs
rgyas dbon gyi gtsug lag khang de nyid du zhabs skor gnang ba'i tshe/ re shig cig nas drung btsun shes rab dpal 'byor bas zhabs phyi la skor ba gnang bas/ skor ba lan
gsum tsam song dus/ ga re gsung nas/ gtsug lag khang sngon gyi thog dpangs phal thog dgu tsam yod pa de la phyag brkyangs nas de'i shing bang yo la phyag reg ste/ 'di ltar
ga bang re re'i nang na yang sangs rgyas kyi sku de bzhin gshegs pa'i ring bsrel gyi snying po can re re dang/ mchod pa cha tshang ba bzhugs pas gsung/ ston pa'i gser
sku 'khyid gang pa dang/ sngon gyi ting rnying pa 'dra la phyag g.yon pa'i mthil du bzhag nas/ g.yas pa'i mtheb mdzub kyis sgra rjes su bskul bar mdzad pa dngos su gzigs
pa las/ ji srid nas bsams pas sku'i rnam par 'phrul pa bstan par yid ches pa'i dad pas snying brlan bar gyur te/ rang gi mched po mchog tu gyur pa drung yigyid chos rgyan
la bshad pas/ khong na re/ rang re'i bla ma 'di'i sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas 'di su zhig gis brjod par spobs/ res rtsom yig drung du byas
dus/ shog logs re tsam phyag thogs med par zhal pad gnang ba de 'bri ba'i ring/ bdag gi snang ngor mnal ba'i rnam pa re gnang bas/ da tshig mtshams ji ltar yod bsam nas mnal
sad phyir smyug mas thag thag bskul bas/ yang sngar gyi de rang gi thad nas sha re bka' stsal zhing/ de lta bu'i sgrib med dag pa'i thugs dang ldan yang/ gzhan ngor thugs
rtsom che ba kun la gal po che'i ched du

gnang nas/ rje btsun 'jam dkar gyi bris thang sman bla don grub pa'i gzabs bris ma chung chung zhig yod pa'i drung du mchod pa gsar pa re bshams/ paN chen nyid kyang re shig
dbu gtums nas thugs dam bzlas brjod kyi tshul re dang/ sha sha dha ra dang/ ri bong 'dzin pa ltar dkar sogs skad gnyis spel ba'i 'jam dkar gyi bstod pa de gsung nas// gang
yin pa'i thugs rtsom la 'jug pa yin no gsung zhing/ chos rje drung btsun pa ni/ ngas bsams na mched po lo tsa ba rang yang sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis bzung ba'i nyan
thos mchog gi tshul 'dzin par ka 'dug/ ding sang sde pa kun gyi yig mkhan 'di dag nyin re bzhin dang/ yi ge'i spor rtsom gyis dus 'da' bar 'dug ste/ tshig re nas len pa'i
sdug brtsir 'di la/ bstan bcos chen po mtha' dag ni thugs rtsom shog logs re lan re las skyor mi dgos pa ya mtshan rmad du byung bar go/ zhes lan brgyar gsungs pa thos
so//der rgya ma nas glang thang du phebs/ dbyar snga ma nas zhal bzhes gnang zhing/ sngar paN chen rin po che mnga' ris su lo gsum bzhugs ring bstud mar ser bas lo tog bcom
pas sngags pa mthu bo ches ser srung la bad dgos pa de la/ da lo paN chen rin po che bzhugs phyin lo gnyer gyis gang byed ces yul mi kun ngag 'cham nas gtad med du bzhag
pas lo dgra'i rnam pa cung zad kyang ma byung bar/ de lo las lo legs pa mi dran pa byung ngo//der dge 'dun tshogs kyi dbu la paN chen rang yang phebs nas/ spyan snga
blo gros rgyal mtshan pa'i drung du thub pa dgongs gsal gyi bshad lung zhang mdo sde dpal ba'i dgongs 'grel dang sbyar ba dang/ logs su paN chen rin po che rang gis gsang
'dus kyi 'grel bshad/ bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i mtha' drug rab

gsal gyi lung gsan no//dbyar ring spyan snga blo gros pas mkhan po dang/ paN chen rin po che'i drung gis slob dpon gnang nas/ thus btsun gtos che ba rang la rab byung gnang
zhing/ mkhas pa chen po lcang ra ba'i drung yang de lo rab byung gnang te mtshan blo gros bzang por btags pas shes so//der tshogs pa rnams dang skye bo grangs med pa la/
'phags pa brgyad stong pa'i bshad lung gzab rgyas gnang zhing/ de dus gnang ba'i brgyad stong pa'i bshad tshoms don bsdu'i gsung rgyun snar thang pa shes rab tshul khrims
kyis yi ger bkod pa'i dpe dngos khong rang gi phyag nas drung btsun bzang po brtan pa'i phyag tu gnang ba khong gis bdag la stsal kyang da lta mnga' ris su lus/ de nas
dpe gzhan ma 'phel bas yid lhag par 'phreng ngo//der grwa gsar slob gnyer ba rnams chos 'khor rtser slob grwa gsar 'dzugs gnang zhing/ dbyar gyi dgag dbye thon rjes glang
thang pa'i che btsun grong chen ma lus pas rang rang gi khyim du spyan drangs nas bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba rgya cher phul zhing/ de skabs grog mkhar nang so la bar brgyud
mdzad/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pas spyan 'dren gnang/ rin chen sgang du grags pa'i stag lung ba'i dgon gzhis nyan po'i mdun der mjal/ bka' 'brel gyi thog mar rje thams
cad mkhyen pa phyogs las rnam rgyal ba'i zhal gzigs kyi dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i rjes gnang de gsan pa'i phyags phyir bdag gi bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pas kyang gsan
zhing/ drung yig chos rgyan pa yang yod ces gsung ngo//de stag lung ngag dbang grags pa dang mjal ba'i sngon ma rang yin/ der stag lung ngag dbang grags pas gos bem ha
hUM ri mo me tog zlum 'dzings

ma khyad du 'phags pa'i na bza' gcig gis gtsos pa'i gnang sbyin yang dpag med stsal zhing/ bka' las da lo khyed kyi dbyar ring 'phags pa brgyad stong pa'i lung mdzad dus steng
gi nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od nyis rim rna cha dgu 'phreng gis bskor ba'i ya mtshan dang rjes 'brel nam mkha' la bltas dus/ lha rdzas kyi me tog dkar po'i char pa sal ma sil
ma babs pa/ de'i ring lam la 'gro mi tshong pa kun gyis kyang mthong bar snang bas nged la zer mi yang yang byung bas yid lhag bsam dag pa byung bas na spyan 'dren zhus
pa yin zhes da lta'i bar du stag lung thang na gtam du sgrog par byed pa las so//de'i don de gtsang phyogs su phebs nas/ de phyin chos grwa chen por chos sgrigs kyi bca'
khrims dgun smal po'i zla ba nas rta zla'i bar/ phar phyin dang mngon pa gong 'og re mos byas tshar re thugs bshad gnang zhing/ dbo dang nag pa zla ba la dpyid chos la/
dbu ma rtsa 'jug rdzogs pa re gsungs/ snron gyi zla ba'i yar ngo'i bco lnga la gso sbyong dang/ dbyar gnas kyi sbyor ba mdzad/ mar ngo'i dga' ba dang po la dbyar gnas par
zhal gyis bzhes nas/ 'dul ba dang tshad ma'i mtha' gcod rgya cher gsung bar mdzad do//de ltar spyi choscho sa? kyi chos tshoms rtsol ba'i ngang nas sgos chos rang rang
gi blo tshod dang bstun pa'i phar tshad spyi TIka/ yan lag rgyas bshad/ don bdun cu/ rtags rigs/ blo rigs/ phar tshad so so'i thal phreng/ thun mong zin thun sbyor ba rtsi
ba'i bar dang/ de las blo tshod gong zhugs la sa skyar tha snyad bzhag pa'i grangs chen bco brgyad du grags pa'i gzhung chen dag gi bshad 'thems/ 'bru gnyer sbyor bas brgyan
pa yang/ paN chen rin po che nyid kyis zur 'chad gang la yang ma bltos par rtsol bar

mdzad de/ dper na nged kyi a jo glo bo dpon drung rnam sras par grags pas/ paN chen dang mjal ba'i skabs/ glo bo nang gi zhib dpyod dris mal gnang dus/ bka' las/ chos rje byams
pa gling pa dpal ldan tshul khrims pa des/ nged rang gi mdun du grangs chen bco brgyad kyi gzhung tshig 'bru sna gcig la yang lhag chad med par spyi TIka rang re'i ngag
las rdzogs shing/ tshig gcig la yang zur ma nyams par bshar sbyang byas/ da ltar rab 'byams pa grags pa can mang dag 'di tsho na yod kyang 'gran dpe med/ sngags kyi ni
tha na bris thig tshun sngar nas shes tshar ba'i byang chub par 'dug pas/ rang re'i dus 'khor dbang mo che'i rdul tshon yang khong gis bzhengs/ de dus lag pa gnyis kas
sa tshon 'bri ba/ sman thang nang pa don grub pas gzigs pa 'di 'dra'i gdod byas na/ nged kyi pir gyis 'bri ba brdzun gsob tu snang/ nged la dngos su zer ba na yang/ mtshan
nyid pa skad 'di chags sngar spun 'tshag che bar snang bas/ khong gis bslabs shes yo nges rdzogs skad sgrog pa snang ngo//sgra snyan ngag sdeb sbyor rnams kyang nged rang
gi lag tshar yin/ phyis slob dpon mi nyag pas khong la rang re'i lag na yod pa'i sgra TIka chen mo'i steng nas sa ris gtong ba skad kyis grags kyang/ de sus su la slob
pa yin ma nges/ rtsis kyang mthar phyin pa lobs 'dug/ mnga' ris su mkhas pa rtsis phrug bya ba'i pha las bslabs zer/ lha ris kyang rgyab tu rtsol med du 'bri shes pa'i grags
pa thos/ khong 'di'i slob gnyer rdzogs pa nas byams glin dbu che ba'i gros bton yin/ ngor tshor lo gsum tsam 'gro dgos par snang/ nged la zhur byung bas de kha legs
khyed rang gis ma shes pa ni bslab rgyu med/ ma thob pa'i dbang lung 'dra yod byas phyis de ka byung 'dug/

na ning nged la yi ge bskur byung ba'i nang na/ sa skya pa gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum blor chud zer ba 'dug/ ding sang sa skya'i bka' 'bum blo la yod pa khong tsam ka yin/ nged
kyang bsam pa rdzogs pas che bkur gyi yig lan byas kyang/ da de lung chung der phangs pa yod de/ bya ba sngon gyi las kyi rang yin par 'dug go// gsung zhes dngos kyis
nged dang sgros byung ba las so//de dus gnang ba'i bka' shog gi nang na yang 'di ltar/dpal ldan shAkya seng ge de'i//gsung rab mtha' yas yi ge'i gzugs//rnam dpyod glegs bur
rab bsdus nas//tshul khrims ske rags mdzes pa can//rdo rje 'chang gi gsang ba la//blo gros goms pa 'dor mdzad khyod//mkhas pa mkhas par yongs shes pa'i//yon tan rgyan
phreng dpag dka' ba//sogs chab shog bka' 'bum nang na 'di las bstod bkur che ba ma gsungs pas mtshan no//de ltar paN chen rin po che nyid kyi zhal lung las/ blo gros yongs
su smin pa'i mkhas pa bgrangs bar mi dpogs pa tsam gyis/ stod mnga' ris/ smad mdo khams/ bar dbus gtsang ru bzhi'i khyon ma lus pa khyab pa'i rnam dkar gyi phrin las yar
ngo'i zla ltar rgya cher 'phel zhing/ de dus srod kyi cha la bsdus sbyor zur rno ba 'ga' re'i zhal spor gnang nas/ nyin rangs rgyal ba'i bka' dang dgongs 'grel gyi don
'chad nyan byas pas/ da lta'i kha 'chal an tsam 'di la sangs rgyas byang sems kyis mi khrel las che yang gsung zhing/ yi ger 'khod pa'i gsung rab kyi nang na yang/kha ba
can du phyis grags pa'i//rdzas dang ldog pa'i bstan bcos ni//'dzin byang kun chub smos ci 'tshal//thos par gyur tshe rna ba dgab//ces gsungs pa ltar shes par ba'o//de nas
sngar gong du brjod pa ltar/ rang

gzhung brtul phod pa'i ring lugs rjes su skyong bar 'dod nas/ dgung lo nga gnyis bzhes pa'i sa mo phag gi lo vc: 1479de nyid la phar phyin gyi spyi don chung ba'i thugs rtsom
gyi dbu tshugs nas/ de'i lo phyi ma lcags pho byi ba'i lo vc: 1480mthar phyin zhing/ 'di skabs bdag gi gnas kyi slob dpon mkhas pa don yod grub pa yang zhabs drung du
phebs pa gnang ngo//der dgung lo nga bzhir phebs pa lcags mo glang gi lo vc: 1481la/ chu mig bdag chen chos dbyings su bzhud pa'i dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa'i khur len/ sku
gdung zhugs 'bul bar gyi bdag gnyer ma lus pa paN chen rin po che nyid kyis lhums zhugs gnang nas/ dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi la ngor dang/ thub bstan rnam rgyal gnyis ka'i
tshogs pa mchod zhing du spyan 'dren gnang zhing/ de dus ngor dgon gsar gyi mkhan stengs na mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje ba bzhugs pa'i dus yin pas/ der phyag gi bkur sti
sogs tshul bzhin gnang zhing/ thub bstan mkhan por mkhas pa chen po go bo rab 'byams pa nyid bzhugs pas der chu mig tu dgon gsum ka'i dge 'dun rnams bsags/ bdag chen drung
gi phyag rdzas rten mchod par 'os pa rnams ngor dang/ rjes byon gyi dpon slob rnams kyi phyag tu btang zhing/ sngon bdag chen zhal bzhugs dus gnang ba'i rdo rje phreng
ba'i dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis ma ding sang ka drug mar bzhugs pa 'di dang/ lam 'bras lha khang gi dar nag la bris pa'i dar gyi/ 'khor chen 'jigs byed rnams kyi dkyil thang
dang gras mthun gyi rdo rje 'chang rnams las gzhan phyag dpe dbang rdzas sogs sna gcig ma lus par tshogs 'gyed gnang bas/ khong la la dag chos rje chen po ba'i drung mtshan
nyid pa sang sang du song bas gsang sngags kyi chas la thugs rtsis mi gnang ba yin yod zer mi yang byung skad do//de dus kyi 'bul yig gi dbur/'khon gyi rigs brgyud 'od
dkar ma nyams shing//mkhyen pa'i cha shas mang po'i mdzod bzung nas//

thugs rje'i bsil zer phyogs brgyar spro mkhas pa//blo gros chos kyi dbang phyug 'di na shar//zhes spel legs kyi snyan ngag kyang paN chen nyid kyis gnang zhing/ der bka' las/
rang re'i pha sgo ma sgo slob dpon sgo// sgo gsum mchod pa'i sku drin can// zer ba de rang yin no gsung/ dus chen la yang mang ja 'bad med stsol ba'i rgyun rje kun dga'
rgyal mtshan pa'i dus kyang yod mod/ phyis nan gyis bcag nas ming mi grag go//de nas dgung lo lnga bcu nga lnga pa'i stengs su rigs gter gyi TI ka'i thugs rtsom gnang zhing/
'di bskul ba po gsang phu'i chen po kun dga' dpal 'byor bas mdzad cing/ 'di la kong ston byang chub sems dpa' dbang phyug grub pa yang thugs lhag par mnyes shing/ zhal
nas/ tshad ma rigs gter 'chad na drung chen po bas mdzad pa'i sde bdun ngag rol 'di dgos par 'dug/ ces yang yang gsung ba paN chen rin po ches kyang snyan du gsan nas/
phyis chos rje kong ston thub bstan gdan sar phebs dus kyang khri ston la/ chos rje kong po rab 'byams pa 'di la dges par 'dug zer gsung sde bdun ngag rol zhig 'bul ba
gnang ngo//chu pho stag lo vc: 1482'di la sde pa gtsang chen pa dang/ hor shAkya ba sogs stobs kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba de rnams kyi bla mar bkur zhing/ phyag dang 'dud pa sngon
du 'gro bas zhabs kyi padmo 'degs par mdzad do//de'i phyi lo chu mo yos lo vc: 1483shar ba'i skabs/ dbus nas mkhan chen nyi ma'i drung dang/ nub chos lung nas kyang
mkhan chen ratna ka ras zhu gsol mdzad nas/ sngar dgung lo zhe brgyad skabs kyi dris lan legs bshad gser gyi thur mar mtshan gsol ba'i lan 'debs kyi bstan bcos kyi thugs
rtsom yang 'bri ba gnang la/ sngar bstan pa'i mes por dgongs nas kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel ba'i drung tshor thog ma'i dri ba phul ba la/ mdzad dka'i dbang las btang snyoms

su gnang nas thugs kha en ma khengs pa'i tshul tsam/ gser thur nyid nas dpes don go bar rnyed/rta thul gyis ni tshangs chen la//'byung chen gang du 'gag dris pas//mes por rlom
pa'i bsnyems pa yis//bden gtam rlung la bskur zhes thos//shes pas mtshon pa'o//gnad kyi don yang/tshad thub 'grel chen bzhi dang gzhung nyid du//tshig zur ji bzhin ma

pa sogs mnga' ris pa 'gas ston bsod snyoms la phyin dus/ stag tshang chos 'khor na sgra pa sher rin pa sku tshe mthar phyin pa'i skabs dang mjal bas/ ding sang chos rje
chen po ba ci mdzad kyi snang gsung ba la/ sngar gyi sdom gsum gyi dris lan de mdzad kyi snang zhus pas/ khong gi gsung gis/ rang re'i de'i dpe zhig btsal bas ma rnyed/ mi
'dra'i ngag nas/rin chen phreng bar gsungs pa yi//zab mo dkrol ba ci la zer//bya ba 'di la nged sgra par tha snyad btags pa'i dbang las 'dri mi mang ba byung la/ 'gyur
khyad dris pa yin// don du bkol ba bya dgos rgyu yin smras/ 'jam dbyangs chen po'i thugs dgongs la/ khong rang gi thugs kha khengs pa'i mkhas pa zhig gis dris pa ji lta'i
lan 'debs yong dgos par snang yang/ ding sang su byed yin/ da 'dri ba'i gnad shin tu brling ba gnang 'dug pas len 'debs dka' ba yod par snang gsung ba'i tshul/ paN chen

gcig/ gser thur nyid

dang bcu gnyis/ dris lan la yang len du spel ba bzhi bdag gi mig gis mthong ste/ tshig zur ma nyams par yid la gnas so//der glo bo nas chos rgyal bkra shis mgon pas thog mar
rin po che'i khu bas gser rkyang du tshar gsum bris shing/ slar par du rko ba'i sbyin gnas kyang gnang ngo//phyis stag lung ngag dbang grags pa'i gzigs lam du gser thur

dbyangs mi gzugs 'jam pa'i dbyangs gang gis//skye nas skye ba nyi shu rtsa lnga'i bar//rjes bzung rjes dpag tshad ma'i blo gros can//sa 'dzin skya ba'i sa skya paN
chen rgyal//rgyal ba'i bstan pa las log tshig dang don//don bzhin gsung rab dpang bzhag mkhas pa'i 'phrul//'phrul chen chos kyi sgo mo brgyad khri dag//dag pa'i thugs su

rab dbyer btags la phyag bgyi'o//dngos bstan gsal dang dngul dkar me long gzugs//mthong bas yid 'dren yongs kyi yid 'jo ba//sbas bshad gting zab rgya mtsho'i nor bu lta'i//dgongs
don dbyings de sngon chad su yis shes//smros shig smra 'dod lce bde 'khyog po can//skad gnyis bsdebs ltar rang mtshan sil bu las//dbu zhabs 'ga' med gnad 'doms

dang bka' yi dgongs 'grel dpang bzhag par//yin min legs par bzhigs tshe gsal bar mthong//gnad dris gnad 'doms gnad nas gzhal ba'i tshe//rang gzhung rang bzhin rang gi bzhed
don rtogs//gzhan zer gzhan bzhed gzhan dang ma 'dres par//bstan bzhin bstan bcos bstan pa'i snying po grub//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo
gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ mkhas pa'i mdzad pa'i mig 'phrul las rjes su bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa bcu bdun pa'o// //Chapter 18: byams mgon
don yod dpal ba dbyings dga' ldan dam par gshegs pa'i skabsder slar yang sdom gsum sa bcad kha skong gi thugs rtsom phran 'ga' yang gnang zhing/ sa 'bri shan 'byed pa'i
bka' drin bla na ma mchis pa'i spobs pa mchog la chos kyi spyan ldan rnams kyi ched du brjod par yang mdzad do//rngog lo'i rnam thar mkhas pa dus mtshungs kyi yi ge yang

ba yang 'di la zer ba lags so// a la la gsung mnga' ris nas phul ba'i ras kyi sku chos rnying pa zhig la phod gzugs gnang nas 'chams mdzad/ der bzhugs gdan la bzhugs nas/

rang re pha spad bka' gros dgos par snang gsung nas

mdzod// rgyab 'di na ja sigs gnyis yod pa la mang ja mdzod/ khyed la mi kun sa skya pa min zer mi 'dug zer bas chos rgyal ma re tshogs su thon mdzod gsung/ da bka' bgros

la thegs nas g.yab ka'i stengs nas tshogs pa zhal bstan nas/ 'o sngon 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis bshums zer bar gda'/ de'i spyan chab las 'phags ma lha mo sgrol ma 'khrungs

ja yang yang zhu ba dang mjal ba

zhig gnang/ de'i dngos gzhi'i skabs su chu dbang dus bum

pa phyag gis bzung nas/ 'an bu'i bla ma theg chen chos kyi rgyal po dbang gnang dus 'di ltar mdzad gsung sku sgeg dang brjid bstan nas gnang zhing/ yang chos rje rdo rje 'chang
chen po 'di ltar du gnang gsung// sku gzugs ci bder mdzad nas bum dbang lan re dang chu dbang lan gnyis gnang/ de dus dbang de gnang ba'i zhing zhing gzhan sbyin bdag
'dra la tshe dbang re tsam gnang zhor la grwa rgan 'gas thob pa tsam las dbang rjes gnang sogs thob pa gtan med/ 'phral gyi byams pa'i mtshan brgya dang/ byams smon gyi

ka dang shangs tshor mi sna 'dra rdzong ba la 'gro/ bsnyung ba'i tshul tsam med pa'i zhing brjes pa 'di ya rang cha 'dug go gsung nas phebs shing/ der bla brang du phebs
'phral drung nas chos kyi pa dang/ drung nas sangs blo ba gnyis de ma thag sku gdung gi drung du mchod 'bul/ byams chos sgrog pa la rdzong ba gnang rjes/ sngar gyi bka'

shangs mthong smon gzhis ka sogs nas/ sku ngo rnam pas gdung mjal gnang ba grub pa dang bstun gsang brtol gyi mang ja 'gyed chas bla brang nas gnang/ dgongs rdzogs gtso
bor bla ma'i gdan sa yin pas gsung/ ngor tshor tshwa ra mang ja dang 'gyed phun sum tshogs pa zhu ba la drung chen sangs rgyas seng ge ba'i phyags phyir ngor pa rang gi zur

la thegs shing/ ngor rang gi tshogs pa kun kyang thugs ma rangs pa dang gzhi byes yo zhal skyengs par

byung/ de'i rjes kyi bya ba rnams dbon po rnam gnyis kyis bsgrubs nas byon/ de gong rje rdo rje 'chang chen gyi dus chen sa ga'i nyer lnga'i stengs su ngor tshor lo re bzhin

gnang/ de skabs grub thob gyi gsung yin pas tig tig ni med/ sngon mi la ras pa'i zhal chems kyi yi ge 'dra ba zhig ka e yod yin na'ang bka' bcag tu mi rung bas/ sku rgyab phyogs

gdung tsha a mo gha shrI'i rtags can gser gyi na bza' stong rwa tsam btab nas phyogs bcur mos rten du bkye/ sku gdung byin rten bzhengs cig e grub lta gsung nas phyag rtags
kyis spras te mchod yul du bzhugs so//sna tshogs smra ba lhur len kha ba'i ljongs//'on thos ngo thon sgrog pa'i gangs can pa//sbyangvc: or: spyang?glang spre'u'i zlos
