pa'i rab tu byed pa bco brgyad pa'o// //Chapter 19: byams pa'i sku'i snang brnyan rjes su bsgrubs pa'i skabsder dpyid sos kyang de la chos dbar sogs ma bteg par/ dgongs
pa'i mthil de 'dis rang rdzogs pa yod gsungs nas de lo'i dpyid chos de lhag par 'chad nyan 'phel ba'i khur len gnang rjes/ shing pho 'brug gi lo vc: 1484dpyid mtshams ring
mo la dpon slob lnga brgya tsam gzhu'i byang lam la mdzad phebs/ de dus rje dus zhabs pa zhing brjes tshar ba'i nang rten sogs la snyan dar sbron pa sogs gnang zhing/
ru dgon sar gyi mkhan po la sku zhang kun dga' snying po bzhugs pa sna dkar rtser gdan 'dren byas/ gzhi la mi bzhugs pas/ phyis paN chen rin po che dang ma mjal gsung nas
thugs khral lhag par che ba gnang zhes par mkhan chos legs pa'i ngag las

kyi tshogs pa lnga brgya posvc: or: po sa?zhag bdun gyi ring la/ karma pa rol pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dbu ma'i gtan tshigs chen po'i gzhi'i khrid gsan dus/ slob dpon nyang
ram pa'i gsung gis/ ga re nged kyi bsam pa la karma pa zer/ ma Ni padma'i lung res mi nor yo sdud pa'i smra bsam brjod med yin snyam pa mthol lo bshags/ 'di na ni ya

ra rigs lung yang de nyid du gnang/

dgag dbye grub nas mkhar rtse glang thang du rim gyis phebs/ spyan snga blo gros pa'i drung dang/ mkhan slob dgung bsgrigs gnang nas sngar gyi kha skong du dmigs pa'i mthus

pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ chos kyi 'khor lo rmad byung bskor ba'i skabs las bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa nyer gnyis pa'o// //Chapter
23: thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tander chos 'khor legs par grub rjes/ dpyid chos stengs su seng ge rtse nas kyi

phogs 'bul dang sgo 'brel/ chos 'khor gyi dga' ston la dmigs pa yin gsung/ gzhir bzhugs kyi dge 'dun yongs la mang ja tshar/ paN chen rin po che'i drung du na bza' cha tshang/
ja sigs/ gos phyi nang sogs drung nas rnam pa bzhi la yang sku zlam re dang dbu zhwa/ bzhugs gding re re/ drung yig chos rgyan dang/ drung chen sangs rgyas seng ge la
ring shag gos stod ma re dang/ gzan re sogs yang dag pa'i 'bul 'degs gnang zhing/ dpyid mtshams ring mo'i dus/ rnam sras kyis ja pa khams pa'i gzugs su sprul nas ja sdum
dpe bral gyi 'bul ba yongs kyi gzigs mthong du phul zhing/ bka' las/ da rang re'i bsam sgo phal pa'i phrin las legs tshogs 'grub pa'i gtang rag tu/ da lo'i dbyar 'di mgon
khang zhig kyang bzhengs gsungs nas/ gur zhal 'khor bcas kyi rten bzo'i dbu 'dzugs pa gnang nyin/ bal po pham mthing tshun 'khor ba'i rnal 'byor pa gcig gis rus pa'i rgyan
drug khyad 'phags shig phul zhing/ rten 'brel lhag par 'grig ces dgyes pa gnang rjes bal po lha bzo ba gcig kyang zhabs drung du byung bas chos skyong gi nang bzhugs
kyi bca' tshul nas bshad pa'i bsgrub dgos kun lhun grub tu byung nas/ bar chad kyi mtshan ma ci yang med par legs par grub ste rab gnas gnang dus/ phyag g.yog rnams la rol
mo'i sgra dbyangs zab pa rang zhig gyis/ zhes bkas bskul nas/ ye shes pa spyan 'dren gnang bas mgon khang gi nang der rlung sogs yong ba'i bug pa gang yang med kyang/ bla
re'i dar sham bskyod pas mar me yang g.yo bar nus pa'i rlung reg bya lhag par tsha ba/ dbyar gyi nyi khyim gyi dus kyi tsha reg lta bu zhig byung nas/ der 'khod pa yo
lus rdul zhing yid lhag par zil che ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang lhan cig rab tu

gnas pa'i gzi byin phebs shing/ de phyin bram ze'i gzugs can de'i sku la/ sngar med pa'i sme ba nag po'i phreng ba star la brgyus pa dang/ sku'i zhal gdong rngulvc: or: rdul?ris
dang ldan pa ltar mi bzod pa'i zil chen rgyas pa 'di byon pa yin la/ de nas de'i dbyar bzhug de rang la shangs nas rnal 'byor dbu legs grub chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan
pa byon te/ paN chen rin po che'i drung du bdag gi nyams snang la kha sang rab gnas gnang ba'i nyin mo dpa ldan sa skya'i bka' srung sde tshogs gser mdog can du 'gro
zer song ba la/ slar dkar bdud lcam dral dang/ dur khrod bdag po gnyis nged la sdod rten cig ma bzhengs 'dug pas log yongs zer byung bas/ rang re'i mgon khang du dkar bdud
dang/ dur khrod bdag po zhig kyang 'bri dgos pa 'dug zhus pas/ de ka bgyi gsung nas/ sman thang pa nang pa lhun grub pas phyag bris su mdzad nas/ dkar mo nyi zla bdud rgyal
thod phreng can/ dpa' bo dur khrod bdag po yab yum rnams gyeng ris su gnang ngo//de'i phyi lo me pho 'brug lo vc: 1496la yang tshogs pa phal che ba la gsung ngag rin
po che gnang zhing/ de grol rjes chos rje 'phrang po ba byon nas/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po nas spyang lung rin po che la brgyud pa'i lam 'bras zhu ba rang la dbus nas
zhabs gtad phebs tshul phul bas/ bka' lung la theg chen lugs kyi lam 'bras yongs rdzogs cha lag tshun rang chos sdings su spyang lung rin po che la thob/ de phyin lam dus
thun bzhi 'chag med byas shing/ de dus tshig 'don de dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i kye rdor mngon rtogs de rang yin pas/ ngor tshor lam 'bras rjes nas zhus dus/ rje
rdo rje 'chang la nged kyi da lta kha bton gyi kyai rdor mngon rtogs 'di bla ma dam pa'i lugs yin pas/ ngor tshor yongs grags bgyid

pa'i mngon rtogs bya bral ma 'di gsar 'dzin dgos lags sam zhus pas/ drung chen po ba rang sngar khyud des rang chog/ nged rang gi rgyun gyi nyams lan yang chos rje bla ma dam
pas mdzad pa 'di steng rang nas lags gsung dngos kyi bka' stsal gnang ba yin/ skyes bu mchog de kun gyi thugs la mtshan 'dzin mi mnga' yang/ nged da lta gtsang phyogs
su grwa sa gsar 'dzugs btab pa 'di la/ mdo kun mkhyen rong ston dang/ sngags ngor pa rdo rje 'chang rang gi gsung rgyun phyag bzhes ma nyams pa rang zhig byed dgos pa'i lugs
gnyis ka'i dam tshig khrel gzhung che bar yod pas/ gser mdog can tsho'i bca' yig tu'ang 'khod/ rang re rang gi thel tshe yang 'byar zin pas sa 'dir ngor lugs las gtan
'chad mi spobs shing/ sngar rgya mar chos sdings dbon po la ni spyang lung rin po che ba'i phrin las rgyun chad dogs rang res gros btab byas nas rdzogs par bshad pa/ de
dus kyang gzhi byes kyi gsol ba 'debs mi mang ba byung kyang gcig la'ang bshad pa med gsung nas zla phyed tsam bka' ma gnang/ de rjes chos rje rab mdo pa rang gis yang yang
nan zhus mdzad pas khong rang dpon slob rnam pa rang la gzhung rkyang gi dmigs pa yod tsam zhig gsang thabs su myur bar gnang rjes/ sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung zhig ched
gtad zhus pas/ drung yig chos rgyan pas spyan chab mdzad nas bkra shis brtsegs par stsal dus/ de'i lo'i chos khrims la da lta'i sa skya las chen ye shes lhun grub pa 'di
yod dus/ bka' lung la/ chos rje 'phrang po bas sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung dgos zer byung bas/ yang yang mi yong khyed rang yang nyon gsung ba la/ bdag chos khrims kyi g.yeng
bas mi 'grub cing/ kha sang grangs chen bco brgyad kyi lung nga la bka' lung thugs la

btags/ sa skya bka' 'bum rang gi mkho zhig mi 'dug lags zhus pas/ ga res sa skyar sdod dgos pa yod/ de dus phyogs shig nas sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung zhu ba'i mi yod pas nyon
gsungs nas gsan zhing/ phyis bdag gis paN chen rin po che nas brgyud pa'i sa skya bka' 'bum gyi lung khong la bzhugs pa'i khungs chod nas snyan bcag 'bul mi brdzangs pas/

rnams kyis gsol ba btab

nas gsung ngag dang rjes 'brel dbyar zhal gyis bzhes pa gnang zhing/ dgag dbye'i rjes la rgya mar spyan drangs/ rab byung bsnyen rdzogs mang du gnang zhing/ 'di lo yang drin
can spyang lung pas lam 'bras tshogs su gsungs pa dang/ logs su chos skyong gur zhal gyi bka' rjes gnang sgrub skor dang/ dga' mo chos mdzad pas zhus pa'i zla la phyag
chen lhan cig skyes sbyor/ lnga ldan/ yi ge bzhi pa sogs kyi khrid gsan gsung zhing/ sngon de myur bar lam gcod gnang nas gser mdog can du phebs shes grag go//de nas phyi
lo vc: 1498sa pho rta lo'i mgo la phar phyin TI ka 'jug sgo gsum pa'i thugs rtsom gnang zhing/ de grub nas dbyar dbang bskur rdo rje phreng ba zla gcig dang zhag lnga'i
ring la rdzogs par mdzad cing/ de skabs rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa sku mched rnams dang/ rje brag dmar ba/ slob dpon rnam pa bzhi sogs bu chen drag rigs rnams dang/ tshogs
pa byin grangs lnga brgya tsam la 'du khang gsar par gnang zhing/ mi nag pa 'dar pa mi bskyod pa yab sras/ sprul sku sman thang pa dang/ rtogs ldan sangs rgyas rnal 'byor

bas chog/ sang de da tsam song dus rdo rje 'phreng ba bskur dgos pa yin no gsung zhing/ phyis de ji lta bar rab gsal zla mgon pa dgung lo bdun cu don gcig bzhes pa/ paN
chen rin po ches rdo rje phreng ba gnang ba'i dgung lo'i chodvc: or: tshod?de rang la bdag gis spyan drangs nas dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe lnga ma'i dbang bskur zhus/ khong
gi sku tshe la dbang gcig po de ka yin zhing/ dbang mi lnga brgya po'i nang nas dbus su paN chen rdor rgyal bas dbang tshar 'ga' gnang ba ma gtogs gzhan gnang mi gcig kyang

brgyud de zhabs drung du phebs/ legs sbyar gyi skad du mchog gi dang

po'i sangs rgyas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang bskur ba zhus te/ mnga' ris glo bor byon/ de dus glo bo na rgya gar gyi paNDi ta si ro ma Ni byon 'dug cing/ khong gi phyag na

steng na glo bo rang gi steng sa chenvc: or: stengs chen?mkhan po byas pa'i chos rje dkon mchog chos skyabs par grags pa/ mi nyag grags rdor ba'i sgra'i bu chen des khas
blangs nas byon pas phyogs kyang ma mtshon par 'dug pa'i skabs der 'dug pas/ paNDi ta rnam pa gnyis kyis sde pa bkra shis mgon la/ khyed rang glo bo yin pa'i lo tsa ba

thugs rtsom

bka'bka drin du mdzad do//de dus 'gro mgon gzhon nu chos bzang pas kyang bka' 'brel gsan pas thugs lhag par mos pas dad pa'i sa la bzhugs pa yin no//de dus nai gu'i khrid skabs

kun spangs rin po che'i gsung sgros nang bstan du gnang ba la/ paN

so//dgung lo don gsum bzhes pa'i lo la yang lam 'bras kyi tshogs chos

rgya cher gnang zhing/ gzhan yang sngags chos phran yang bde mchog lu hi pa'i dbang dang bskyed rdzogs/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i lus dkyil dang 'brel bar dril bu rim lnga'i khrid/
bde mchog dkar po'i byin rlabs khrid dang bcas pa rje brag dkar dmar gyis zhu ba po gnang nas rim par stsal zhing/ rje sems dpa' brag dkar ba'i drung gting skyes tshor

nas sems dpa' chen po'i drung du gser mdog can du gsung ngag gsan nas tshur phebs skabs/ bkra shis

du bzhengs pa mdzad stsal ba de las gzhan gcig kyang ma gnang zhing/ rje rin po che brag dmar ba'i drung gis kyang paN chen rin po che nyid la gsan des dgongs pa thugs la
bzhag nas/ sdom gsum rin chen spungs par ma brgyud bde mchog gi skabs su brgyud pa yang rdo rje 'chang/ stag lung bka' bzhi pa rin chen bkra shis/ paN chen rin po che las
zhes bkod kyang/ rjes nas gtan gsan ma thub par phyis zha lu mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims pa las gsan pa yin no//dam pa'i chos bzhin spyod pa'i bka' srung che//dam
tshig can gyi chos skyong 'khor bcas rnams//dam can ma lus vc: letter r/'a preceding this syllabledus pa'i pho brang na//dam bcas tshul bzhin dgongs pa'i dbyingsdbying
sa na bzhugs//rnam mang skye dgu'i chogs rnams tshim mdzad pa'i//rnam dkar 'phrin las yongs la mngon gyur cing//rnam grangs du ma'i mdzad pa'i legs byas ni//rnam dag rgyal
ba'i bstan pa rgyas phyir lags//grags pa bsam yas 'dzam gling sa yi khyon//grags pa'i rnga chen sgra yis khyab byas nas//grags pa don mthun chos can dag pa yi//grags pa'i
ba dan dkar po spel bar mdzad//rgya gar gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi tas//rgya yig legs sbyar skad du bkod pa'i phreng//rgya gar yul nas 'ongs pa'i rnal 'byor'byer pas//rgya
gar 'khor tshe gang gi drung du phul//chos las brtsams pa'i nyin mtshan mdzad pa'i tshogs//chos bzhin spyod pa'i 'khor 'bangs slob mar bcas//chos kyi rjes 'brangs dad
pa'i sa thob dag//chos kyi rgyal po gang gi zhabs pad mchod//

ngag gi dbang pos rjes bzung mkhas pa'i phul//ngag dbang gsung gis 'gro blo'i mun sel ba//ngag tshig sdebs legs yongs kyi yid 'dren pa'i//ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs bla
ma rgyal//mkhyen rab mthar phyin shes bya'i gnas rnams la//mkhyen pa'i dpal gyis mi shes mun sel gang//mkhyen ldan lo chen mchog gis nyer dgongs nas//mkhyen yangs sa lo
de la legs par bsnyad//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan
las bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa nyer gsum pa'o// //Chapter 24: gzur gnas kyi mkhas pa dges pa'i skabsde nas dgung lo don bzhir phebs pa lcags mo bya lo'i dpyid chos vc:
1501yan la/ mdo phyogs kyi dbu tshad chos 'byung tsam ma gtogs pa'i gsung rtsom phal cher grub cing/ yi ge rang gi steng nas lung bshad rdzogs par stsal/ rtog ge'i snying
po glo bo chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan pas par gyi sbyin bdag mdzad/ kun bzang rol mtsho gu ge chos rje rnam rgyal bas sbyin bdag gnang bas mtshon pa'i lung snying/
kun las btus kyi dka' 'grel/ 'dul ba'i bslab bya chen mo/ dbu ma'i stong thun/ lugs gnyis rnam 'byed rtsa 'grel gyis mtshon pa'i bar rnams kyang rang rang gi dad brtson gyis
legs par bsgrubs te/ dper na dbu ma'i stong thun chen mo bya yul du gting skyes rab 'byams pa/ drung nas sde bdun pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan pas bsgrubs pa'i par byang
'byung ba ltar dang/ par phal cher gyi par byang yang paN chen rin po che nyid kyis gsung rtsom du gnang ba yin te/ rtog ge'i snying po'i 'jug na sgrub pa dang ni sun
'byin gyi//gnas rnams legs par thugs chud nas//tshul bzhin 'doms mdzad tshad ma yi//

mkhan po yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas//de nas phyogs kyi glang po yis//don de 'jam dpal dbyangs la gsan//phyogs glang gzhung brling rtogs dka' ba//gsal bar 'chad mkhas grags
pa'i mtshan//gzhung rtsom gzhan la ma grags pa//rngog los gsal bar bshad ces gsung//bod kyi rgan po'i lugs dor ba//sa skya'i 'jigs med dpa' bos bshad//sngon mas gsal bar
ma bris shing//phyis 'byung gtam gyis ma sbags par//rtog ge'i mtsho nas brda chad kyi//snying po bsdus pa'i dpag bsam 'di//gang gi rnam dpyod skyed tshal du//dge bar gshin
zhing shis gyur pa//rje btsun blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal//bzang po'i bka' dang de nyid kyi//'byor pa'i bang mdzod nas byon pa'i//zhes sngon dang da lta'i gnas ma lus pa'i
gnas don bde blag tu rtogs par byed pa sha stag 'byung ngo//gzhan phyogs glang chos grags kyi rtogs brjod/ gzhi gsum cho ga/ bya pas gser thur la dris pa'i lan 'debs
sogs gsung rtsom phra mo'i par kyang mang du spel lo//dngos bstan bstan bcos su ma 'khod par gzhung tshig rang gi stengs su bka' stsal gyi bshad pas gtan la phab pa'i tshul
rnam thar gnyis su zur tsam yang ma smos 'dug la/ rnam thar ma ti mar grangs su btab pa ni 'di ltar/ 'phags pa brgyad stong pa slob dpon seng ge bzang po'i brgyad stong
'grel chen dang bcas pa/ sdud pa/ 'dul ba me tog phreng rgyud rje rong ston chen po'i TIka'i stengs dang/ yang de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dbu ma'i stong thun/ bslab spyod
gnyis/ dpa' bo'i skye rabs/ theg bsdus/ mdo sde rgyan/ rgyud bla ma/ dbus mtha' rnam 'byed rnams kyi 'grel pa/ dbu ma tshig gsal/ ye shes snying

po'i bden gnyis/ jo bo'i lam sgron/ gtam bya rin chen phreng ba/ bshes spring/ phya bsdus/ rigs gter rang 'grel/ rma bya byang brtson gyi dbu ma'i stong thun/ thub pa dgongs
gsal/ 'dul ba'i gleng 'bum dang/ bu ston chos 'byung rnams la yang zhu ba po so so'i ngor bshad lung yang dag stsal lo zhes 'byung ngo//bya'i lo vc: 1501'di la bla ma'i
sku'i dkyil 'khor me long la gzugs brnyan shar ba ji lta ba'i sku 'dra yid bzhin nor bu yang bsgrub par mdzad cing/ 'di'i nang bzhugs sogs kyi nges gnas drung yig chos rgyan
pas yi ger 'god pa gnang ba las shes par bya'o//de nas chu pho khyi lo vc: 1502dgung lo dong lngar phebs skabs/ sgra pa grags pa blo gros pa dpal sdings nas 'bras yul
du/ byang pa bdag mo tshe ring mas spyan drangs pa'i yar lam mjal du phebs pa la dri mal gnang bas/ sgra'i phyogs la phul du phyin pa'i mkhyen pa mnga' bar legs par dgongs
nas/ paN chen rin po che nyid kyis kyang lung dang mthun pa tsandra pa'i sa ris khong la gsan par bzhed de bka' stsal gnang bas sgra'i glegs bam gnyis phyag tu bzhag
nas/ 'bras yul nas byung ba'i 'bul nor rnams skyel ba dang/ slar yang sgra'i dpe nyer mkho 'dra len pa la 'byon zhus pas/ mi gnang ba las drung nas rang sku na tshod bgres
pa tshun lam la 'o brgyal zhing/ rin chen chos kyang dkon la rtag tu 'tshe ba'ang mang// yin pas bar chad du yang 'gyur srid pas gtan mi legs gsung kyang/ dngos po rnams
thugs kyis ma dpogs pas skyel ma la byon/ der chibs dpon shAka bzang chibs skyel dang/ slar chibs bsu la gnang zhing/ sgra pa grags blo bas khong rang gi phyag rdzas rnams
thel 'byar yang dag gi gnyer cag mdzad rjes/ sang shar la 'byon rgyu'i do nub skas la 'byol bas rkyen

byas blo bur du gshegs nas/ chibs slar log/ tshul phul bas thugs khral cher gnang zhing/ tshogs su mang skol dang bsngo ba rgyas par gnang zhes thos so//de mtshams dbyar chos
rgyal lhun po nas rgyal ba'i dbang po karma pas bka' shog gnang/ der nyi ma dbus gtsang gi phyogs la rta kha bsgyur yod pa yin pas/ bstan pa la phan pa'i gros 'dri 'dra
snang ba la dbus phyogs su myur bar 'byon pa dang/ dbu tshad kyi chos 'byung de rtsom la bskur mdzod gsung ba'i bka' lung phebs don la/ dbus la lan rjes ma dpon slob nyung
bsdus rang phebs pa'i skabs/ chos 'khor lha sar rgyal dbang karma pa dang mjal nas/ lugs gnyis ka'i nges gsang dpag med gnang rjes/ glang thang dang rgya ma rnams su
yul tsam zhabs kyis bcags/ skal ldan rnams la dbang dang byin rlabs sgo du mas rgyud smin cing grol bar mdzad/ lhag par dga' mo chos mdzad pas snga res phebs skabs lam zab
gsag sbyangs zhus nas nam mjal maNDal 'bul ba ma chag pa'i gdung shugs 'bul ba gnang ba la/ de res lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs glang ri thang gi gzims
khang gsar pa dge 'phel du stsal bas gro yun cig yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin bzang po la 'byams shing/ paN chen rin po che'i bka' las kyang/'o zab mo'i lam gyis byin gyis
brlabs pa'i tshe//rje btsun bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs su gzigs//skad cig gcig la chos rnams thugs su chud//thugs grol khyod la spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo//zer ba'i dpe de
de ring gi 'di red do zhes/ drin can spyang lung pa dngos kyis gsan nas bdag la bka' lung du gnang ngo//de rjes chos rje stong rab shAkya bzang po bas gsol 'debs su gnang
nas/ drin can spyang lung pa'i drung sogs dbang cha gcig la kye rdo rje

rgyu lam/ lam zab bir srungs/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs stsal rjes/ rgya ma dge slong ma'i drung gis zhus nas snying po don gsum gyi khrid gnang zhing/ 'pho ba'i skabs
stod ra ba la dngos su 'pho ba 'thebs tsam gyis brgyal thabs su gnas pa la/ drung yig chos rgyan pas dbu gtsugs nas brdung ba gnang zhing/ snyan la zhal gtad de 'bod
pa gnang bas ji zhig nas thugs dran rnyed byung zhes dngos su gzigs pa'i gsung sgros drin can spyang lung pa'i zhal las thos so// 'di dbus phyogs su bka' chos gnang ba'i
rjes mar snang ngo//der dro sa'i la rtse bar skyel thung la zhal slob drag pa yos phebs shing/ der dga' mo chos mdzad pas bdag nyin re bzhin ja 'thung ba la ja mchod bdag
rang gi bla ma rnam gsum gyi mtshan thon pa zhig zhu zhes gsol ba btab pas/ da lta'i ja mchod rnam shes ma 'di de phral ja gral der drung yig chos rgyan pa la zhal sbror
gnang zhing/ thog ma la ngag dbang grags pa'i zhal du/ de nas paN chen mkhas pa'i zhal du/ de nas thar pa'i rgyal mtshan zhal du gsung ba yod/ drin can spyang lung pas gsan
pa'i bka'i bdud rtsi'i mtha' yang 'di nyid yin no// zhes bya mchod mdzad res kyis gsung ngo//yar lam dbyar gyi chu mgo rgyas pa'i dus kyi chu lud pa zhig dang thug ste/
khal gyis lam ma bgrod par mtshoms skabs/ paN chen rin po che'i zhabs drung phebs/ der ram pa sogs kyi la bskor ba min pa mi thar nges pa'i tshul phul bas/ a'u rtsi 'dengs
gsung nas phebs ma khad rang chu thog so gsum re blo bur du bri nas sgal tshas kyi sne tsam yang ma bangs par 'phrang la phebs skabs 'phral/ sngar ltar chu sngar shul
du 'phel ba'i grub rtags gnang/ der gser mdog can du dbyar gnas mdzad cing/ mtshan brjod kyi TI ka'i bshad

pa sogs bka' chos phran bu 'ga' dang/ mi nyung bsdus la sbyor drug gi khrid cig stsal zer ro//de nas dgung lo don drug bzhes pa'i dus vc: 1503/ tshes bco lnga zhig gi nyin
rnam sras ser chen gyi rjes gnang gnang grab la/ rje dbon shAkya rgyal mtshan pa'i drung dang/ da lta'i a zhang bsod lhun pa sogs dbus nas phebs pas/ de 'phral mjal ka gnang
zhing/ de'i nyin rnam sras rjes gnang yang gnang bas/ drung chen dpal dar bas paN chen rin po che'i drung du rje dbon?dpon pas thog mar rnam sras gsan pa'i rten 'brel
gyis rnam sras bran du 'khol ba zhig yod lags sam zhus pas/ ci cha dbon chung rnams sras phyi la khrid pa zhig ni yod red gsungs pas/ de dus khong dag gi blo yul du rnam
sras phyi bzhin du byon pa'i go ba byas kyang/ da lta bsam dus nor lha phyir khrid gsung bar snang bas/ gser mdog can bla brang gi khyad nor rnams dbus kyi glang thang gi
phyogs su phyir skyel gnang ba'i ma 'ong lung bstan du sems so//der gnas kyi slob dpon drung nas lha btsun pa'i drung du bcol dam gnang bas sngar dbus su yang chen por
'phyur ba'i drung bsdus ra sogs brda sbyar tsam gnang ba'i sne mthud pa'i thugs gnyer ma mthud gnang zhing/ lo de'i dpyid chos la dpon sa bdag mo chen pos chos dbar gnas
gsar du bteg pas rje dbon shAkya rgyal mtshan pas gtso mdzad mnga' ris pa hor rab 'byams pa sogs la chos dbar sar du 'brum pa byung na'ang/ nyes skyon gcig kyang ma byung
bar legs par thar ba 'ba' zhig byung ngo//der grwa pa byings gser mdog can du log/ paN chen rin po che'i zhabs phyir drung nas nyang raM pa dang/ paN chen rdor rgyal ba
grwa shar du yod pa cig kyang phyags phyir khrid nas rtse chen du phebs/ tshe dbang sogs bka' chos mang ba

gnang ba zhing/ rtse chen du gnam lcags kyi thog byung ba yang thugs rje'i mthus nyes skyon gang yang ma byung tshul gzigs gsal gyi thugs rgyus steng nas 'di thad rnam thar
rdor rgyal mar zhib tu bkod 'dug go//de nas dbyar bzhugs dgagnggag dbye grol rjes/ rin spungs su rje thams cad mkhyen pa zhwa nag cod paN 'dzin pa rgyal dbang chos grags
rgya mtsho ba'i spyan sngar phebs/ zla gcig tsam gdan chags shing/ phyogs ris kyi 'dus pa'i dge 'dun lung rigs smra ba ma lus pa'i rtsod pa'i dpang por bzhugs shing/ rgyal
ba'i dbang po nyid kyis mdzad pa'i tshad ma'i rigs gzhung rgya mtsho'i dpe stsal nasdag byed mdzod ces bka' bsgo ba gnang bas/ nyin mtshan du thugs g.yengs ches pas gzigs
skabs ma byung bar de dus phyags phyir mkhas pa don yod pa yang bzhugs pas/ phyag dpe stsal nas gang gzhan lugs 'dres pa'am khyad thon gyi zur cha gang 'dug la shog gzer
thob shog/ ces bka' gnang ba ltar mdzad nas phul bas/ zhogs pa'i yud tsam gzigs pas zhag 'ga'i bar du rigs gzhung rgya mtsho las brtsams pa'i bshad pa kho nas dus 'da'
bar mdzad rjes/ sngar rgyal dbang karma pa nyid kyis bkas bskul ba'i dbu tshad kyi chos 'byung rnams phyag tu bzhes nas 'dus pa'i dbus der re re nas dri mal gnang ba la/
'phros pa'i zab bshad 'ba' zhig pas zla ba tsam gyi yun 'da' bar mdzad/ 'di skabs kong ston byang chub sems dpa'pa dbang phyug grub pa dpal bzang po yang karma pa mjal
ba la byon yod pas der paN chen rin po ches bshad pa gnang res bzhin slob ma gus ldan slob dpon gyi bshad 'doms nyan pa'i tshul bzhin du gsan ces rang gzhan gyi chas bsdus

pa'i gral la 'khod pa kun gyis sgrog cing/ de nas slar gser mdog can gyi chos grwa nyid du phebs nas dgun chos kyi dus chos skyong bar mdzad skad do// //sngon rab mkhas pa
yongs kyis ma gzigs pa'i//legs bshad gzhung tshig la gnas mngon sum pa//chos spyan yangs pas phra rgyas spu ris kyang//ma 'dres gsal ba'i yul du legs par dgongs//rang bzhed
lung dang rigs pa'i dmag dpung gis//gzhan zer lung rigs ltar snang sun phyung ba//khyod kyis legs smras mkhas pa'i kha rgyan gyis//bstan bcos gang de bstan pa'i nor rdzas
nyid//rgyal ba'i bka' dang dgongs 'grel bstan bcos dag//gzhung tshig yi ge nyid la rab dpyad nas//'di de'i dgongs pa 'di lta nyid yin zhes//bden gsungs ljags las dag
gsal 'doms par gsungs//karma par grags bdun pa'i bka' yi 'phrin//rab chags thugs rje'i lcags kyus yongs bskul bas//yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i khur khyer glang po khyod//srid
dang zhi ba'i phun tshogs dbus der byon//bshad mkhas gang gis chos don sgrar bsnyad tshe//nyan mkhas snying la zim char bzhin du 'bab//smra mkhas yongs kyis ched du sgrog
pa'i gzhi//brjod mkhas don bzang rgyal ba'i bka' dang mtshungs//khyod gsung legs bshad lha yi rnga bo che//thos pas ma rig gnyid las rab bslang zhing//rab snyan lha rdzad
pi waM gling bu'i sgra//yun ring rna ba'i lam nas snying dbus bzhugs//tshig dang don du bcas pa'i nges gsang ni//rgyal ba'i chos rnams yongs kyi bcud bsdus pa//gcig shes
kun grol 'chad mkhas 'phrul gyi sgo//dus der legs lam sgo brgya dbye bar mdzad//ces paNDi

ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ gzur gnas kyi mkhas pa dges pa'i skabs las rjes su bsgrags pa'i
rab tu byed pa nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa'o// //Chapter 25: yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i skabsde nas dgung lo don bdun du phebs pa shing pho byi ba'i lo vc: 1504/ gzhan snang
du chab gzhi la brten pa'i bsnyel ba'i tshul ston pa gnang skabs sde bdag so so'i phyag rtsa 'dzin pa'i 'tsho byed sman grong pa dang/ bo dong 'tsho byed pa sogs mkhas
pa rnams zhabs drung du mngags nas gsol sman zhu ba sogs kyi 'phrod bsten gnang yang cher sku khams la dngas bskyed ma byung bar dbus phyogs su grongs sgra chen po byung
zhing 'tsho byed rnam pa yang sku nas dang bstun pa'i/ da ste gsol ba thebs pa dka' zhes yid khong du chud pa las/ slar sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis rlobs par mdzad de/
gzhan ngor rlung sbyor la brten pa'i thugs ka'i thad nas chab chu rnams mngon sum du phyir bsal nas/ mod la sku zo mdog bde ba'i dpal 'dzin pa gnang bas yongs kyi yid sos
shing/ zhal dkar ba'i bsnyungs dngas 'bul mi stod mnga' ris nas bzung ste dbus gtsang gi bar gyi dkon nor dpag med kyi me tog dbul bar byas so//der paN chen rin po che nyid
kyi spyan snga bar gyur ba'i drung nas lo tsa ba dharma dhra dza yang de lta bus thugs bskul nas rgya gar rdo rje gdan bskor ba la gshegs te/ de phyin mnga' ris bzhi
sde pa gzims dpon rnam rgyal bas spyan tshab kyi phyags phyi gnang zhing/ drung yig chos rgyan pa rgya gar la gshegs phyin/ dus 'khor gyi phyi nang gzhan gsum dang/ bde mchog
gi rnam bshad dang po'i sangs rgyas rab tu grub pa'i zhal lobs kyi yi ge pa yang da lta'i a zhang par grags pa 'dis gnang bas/ bstan bcos 'di dag gi mjug na yi

ge ba ni bsod nams ye shes lhun grub po zhes 'byung bas mtshon la/ de dag gi skabs su rje brag dkar dmar gnyis kyis sngags chos zhu ba po gtso bor gnang nas/ rje brag dmar
bas 'di skabs sdom gsum rin chen spungs pa'i thugs rtsom ri bo gser sdings kyi ngogs yangs dben gnas yang dgon rtser mdzad cing/ rje sems dpa' brag dkar bas chos mtshan brgya
rtsa brgyad kyi zhu ba po gnang nas dpal gyi mgur las nyer 'doms su yi ger bkod pa'i bka'i bsdu ba yang 'di yan gyis yongs su grub bo//shing mo glang lo vc: 1505dgung
lo don brgyad bzhes skabs/ sde pa sgar pa'i drung sogs sa chen skyong ba'i stobs kyi rgyal po chen po dag la dbang khrid du ma'i chos kyi bdud rtsi stsol zhing/ gdul bya'i
yul dag la yang mdo dang sngags kyi chos kyi char chen po dus rgyun chad med par bka' drin du mdzad bzhin pa'i skabs nas/ 'brong sgang bsam grub rtse/ seng ge rtse rnams
su zla phyed tsam de'i ring phebs bzhud gnang ba la yang thugs mi longs pa'i rnam pa gnang zhing/ slar 'phral la rang log nas gser mdog can du phebs ma thag blo bde'o
zhes/ dus rgyun ldan du bka' lung byon zhing/ mdo sngags kyi 'chad nyan rgya chen gyi ngang nyid nas thugs dam gyi rim pa chu bo'i rgyun gyi rnal 'byor la skad cig kyang
g.yel ba med par snga dgongs kyi thun gtor gyi bar nyin gcig tsam yang 'chag pa'i skabs mi srid par dus 'khor mor gnang zhing/ srod chen la kRaShaN sa ri'i rwa dung cig
bus/ gu gul gyi dud pa chen po cig btang ba nas/ sang nam ma langs par gzim chung du su yang mi 'gro ba snga mo man gyi phyag srol yin zhing/ sngar gos sku bzhengs man la
nub mo phyag rnga yang brdung gnang zhes sgrog la/ phyag rnga la me 'bar ba'i cho 'phrul drung chen sangs rgyas seng ges gzigs shes rnam thar rdor rgyal mar bris gnang zhing/
rgyun du DA dril yun rings gnang/

bka' las kyang/ DA ma ru 'khrol dus na/ mkha' 'gro ma gtso/ mkha' 'gro ma tsho/ dur khrod gnas su e 'gro mi 'gro/ 'gro na 'gro 'gro na da 'gro zer ba zhig dgos pas yong gi
e gnang gsung zhing/ brtags na de nyid kyi sgra kho nar 'byung zer ro//der myur du dga' ldan la bskyod par dgongs pa'i/ bya rgod phung por tshogs pa kun la yang/ nged rang
gis dkor de snga mo nas zos pas kha po de 'don long mi yong bsam pa byung/ don gsum lon nas kha po de 'don byas nas kyang lo kha yar song/ lo brgya yar mar gyi mkhas pa
so so'i bzhed ma 'dres pa'i shan 'byed de thub rang dgos pa yin/ phyis gang lab 'tshor chas su byas ngo sor sgrog/ de las gzhan pa sa skya pa ma yin pa skad byed pa'i chos
skad zur bzhag cig yod skad kyi sdang smras byed/ chos spyod shlo ka cig 'don mi 'don gyis sa dge'i dbye byed byas rang tshugs thub pa cig dkon snang ngo//rang res dum
re smras kyang grog po 'di'i 'bum chung yan chad du ka yin/ yin kyang snga mo nged rang kyi 'dod pa su gang gis kyang ma 'khyor ba la/ da 'khyor ba de dga' rab 'khyor gyi
'dug/ nged rang gi lta grub 'phyugs zer mi 'dug kyang/ de tsam cig 'phyugs ma 'phyugs kyi rnam dpyod sbro rgyu yod/ don du gtugs na mna' skyel pher ba yod do gsung zhing/
rang re lo 'di dang 'di la gnas 'di dang 'dir phyin/ bla ma 'di dang 'di la chos 'di dang 'di zhus shes sngar yi ger bkod pa'i don bsdu ljen par gsung/ de dus kyi mnga'
ris pa blo gsal ba mang po las thos tshod gong du thad sor bris pa'o//de ltar zhib par gsungs nas 'di 'dra yang sems la nges dgos phyogs gar shed du phyin dus/ mis drung

mi yong zhus pas/ min gsung/

'o na ci lags zhus pas/ 'od gsal zer ba de yin par snang ngo// ngo shes dgos pa yin gsung zhing/ der gtor shom da lta rang gyis shig gsung ba'i lugs ltar bshams nas rgyas par
'bul ba gnang/ sngags phyag rgya ting nge 'dzin nan sbyor du mdzad rjes/ seng ge'i nyal stabs kyis en tsam gzims pa'i tshul bstan/ de las bzhengs nas bo dong 'tsho byed
pas phyag rtsa cig zhus pas/ rtsa de ma bsdus snang ngam gsung ba la/ cher mi rtogs pa 'dug lags zer/ phyag 'bul zhig byas nas gsol ja sang tsam zhig bzhes e spro zhu ba
la/ de ka bgyi gsung nas/ gsol ja thon byung dus/ gzims dpon rnam rgyal bas gsol dkar bteg nas zhal hub gang gsol nas de bsdus gsung ste/ sku bsrang phyag gnyis sa gnon
mnyam gzhag gnang/ dgongs pa mngon du mdzad de chos kyi dbyings su snyoms par zhugs pa'i de ma thag/ rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas nyang stod nas lam bsrangs phebs pas/
drung chen sangs rgyas seng ges nan du spyan drangs/ phyag mdzad sku mdun du bzhugs pas spyan cer gzigs byung/ bka' lung gzhan ni ci yang mi gsung/ der rje kun dga' rgyal
mtshan pas kyang/ sku drung du bzhugs nas thugs dam lam dus shig len pa gnang ba yin zhes thos so//kye ma 'dzam gling sa yi ljongs 'dir ni//thub pa'i skyes mchog lan gnyis
'da' tshul bstan//rgya bod gdul bya'i yid bde'i dpal 'phrog pa'i//brtse ldan khyod las khros pa srid 'dir su//thub bstan mkha' dbyings gsal ba'i klongs yangs 'dir//bstan
'dzin rgyu skar 'char nub mang na yang//yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i nyi zla khyod gshegs nas//'dzam gling gnam sa ma lus mun pas khyab//mgon khyod mgon med 'gro 'di yongs
dor na//

dga' gnas dga' ldan zhing der dgongs pa'i tshe//sgra bsgyur sgra tshad tshul rig lo tsa ba//yid 'byung yid skyo'i ngang nas rgya gar bzhud//lha mi'i gtsug rgyan 'jam dbyangs
zhing 'pho la//lha dbang 'chi ltas mthong ltar rab skrag ste//lha yi btsun pa shA ra dwa ti'i bu//lha mchog shAkya'i rgyal po'i sngon la thegs//gangs can skal med rmongs
pa spyi brtol can//smra mkhas mchog gi nyi ma 'das zin gyi//lha ngan 'ug skad mi srun srin bya'i tshogs//'bad de rang skad sgrog la gad mo byos//ston pa'i bstan pa 'dus
nad gzer bu can//'tsho byed sman pa'i rgyal pos ring spangs pa//bshad bsgrub zung zad srog gi lhag ma khyod//'gro 'di'i bde skyid dag dang lhan cig gum//nyi tshe'i thos
sbyangs yus dag mkhas pa'i tshogs//bstan pa'i tshig don dpyod pa'i khur med kyis//sangs rgyas las lhag blo gros cher rlom des//smra brjod 'chad rtsod rang dran lhur long
shig//ces paNDi ta chen shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i skabs las bsgrags
pa'i rab tu byed pa nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'o// //Chapter 26: phrin las kyi 'khor lo rgyun mi chad pa'i skabsder thog mar gsang thabs kyis sku rim du ming btags pa'i mang skol
bstud mar gnang rjes/ gsang brtol dang rjes 'brel mi dbang chen po sgar pa'i drung yang phebs nas gdung mjal sogs gnang zhing/ sku gdung gi chas 'bul mi kun gyi spyan
lam du gsang ba'i gnas ltar mi mngon pa dang/ dbu'i gtsug tor mchog tu 'phags pa sogs gsal bar rtogs shing/ gdung las 'phro ba'i 'od zer gyis mchod pa bshams pa'i mar me'i
'od zil gyis gnon pa/ mkhas pa sangs 'od pa de dus sku gdung drung na byams chos klog sgrogs

la bzhugs pas dngos su gzigs shing/ der sde bdag drung gis bkas bcad/ sku gdung yid bzhin dbang gi rgyal po nyid ril po gcig tu bzhugs pa'i bzhugs gnas dngul gdung bkra shis
sgo mangs ma grub bar shing sgam du dar zab dri bzang gis bkur sti gnang/ gdung 'bul phyogs bcu nas byung ba dang/ gzhir bzhugs kyi zhal bzhugs ma lus pas dgung zhag so
so dang/ gsang phu/ nA lendra/ glang thang/ rgya ma chos sdings sogs bsgrub 'os kun tu dgongs pa'i dbyings yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i 'phrul rgya chen gnang zhing/ gdung
zhag khongs su bkra shis brtsegs pa'i chos rje rdo rje 'chang dang/ kun mkhyen rong po'i sku 'dra dang grangs mnyam gyi gser sku 'di bzhengs pa'i lugs gtong dus/ drung
chen sangs rgyas seng ges paN chen nyid kyi dbu skra bubs cig lugs khar btab pas/ lha bzo ba'i bal po ha las bzhin dngang skrag dang bcas blug pas/ 'drangvc: or: 'drad?phyis
kyang 'phul mi dgos pa 'dra ba'i 'ja' 'od 'khyil ba zhig byung zhing/ sprul sku sman thang pas sngar paN chen rin po che rang gis phyag bzhengs gnang ba'i rngog lo'i
rnam thar zhing bkod/ rje rong ston la bzhes gnyen dam pa bcu phrag bzhis bskor ba/ kun mkhyen don yod dpal ba'i sku 'dra bka' 'brel zhus pa'i bla ma ma lus pas bskor ba
rnams dang dras mnyam de bris so//der dgung zhag kun dang lhag par tshe bco lnga yin no cog la me tog gi char gsal bar babs so//der rgyal ba gnyis pa'i sku'i snang ba nub
nas/ slar dad mos kyi mig rkyen ni sngar dgung lo'i thad so so rtsom pa'i phreng ba spel ba ltar bka'i glegs bam 'di dag nyid yin pa'i phyir/ bdag nyid chen po sangs rgyas
dngos byon gang gi rjes su 'brang ba'i yi dam mchis na thams cad mkhyen pa gang gi gsung

gi bdud rtsi 'di rnams la nan tan gyis lta zhing kun chub par bya ba nyid las 'bad pa'i gnas med do// zhes nges par bya ba'i phyir nyung ngu'i tshig tu bsdebs nas brjod pa
'di ltar/blo gsal smra ba'i ngag gi dpal ster rig gnas phra mo'i legs bshad tshogs//sngon rabs shes byed bla ma'i yon tan rgyan phreng spel ba'i rnam thar dang//de de ji
bzhin bshes gnyen dam pa'i yon tan brjod pa'i bstod pa'i tshig//rang gi mdzad pa'i ngo mtshar ston pa'i deb gter bstod pa'i rab byed bzhi//rgyal dang de sras mchog la bsngags
pa'i snyan ngag mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog dang//gzhan gyis brtsad cing dris pa'i rgal lan sprin yig sna tshogs spel ba'i sde//sngags gzhung zab dgu'i bcud bsdus sdebs legs
rang gzhan 'byed pa'i brda gsang gang//lhag pa'i lha mchog brnyes pa'i sgrub thabs sngags 'bru shes byed sgo du ma//tshad ma'i chos 'byung dpyod ldan dga' byed dka' 'grel
rigs pa'i snang ba 'phro//rtog ge'i 'khrul pa yongs su 'joms byed rtog ge'i snying po bsdus pa'i bcud//sde bdun rigs pa'i gter gyi rol mtsho sde bdun bang mdzod lde mig
can//sems tsam gsal ba'i me long gang der shes bya'i gzugs brnyan ma lus shar//bzhed tshul rgya mtsho'i rlabs kyi 'phreng bar rgya bod mkhas pa'i 'grel tshul bstan//lus
dang yan lag rgyas par 'chad byed lung don rgya mtsho'i gting mtha' yas//gzhung tshig re re sbyor ba'i TI ka gnad kyi sgron mes gsal bar byas//rang gzhung sgrub pa'i lung
rigs rgya mtsho legs bshad rba klong g.yo ba can//zur 'debs chu chen rnam pa bzhi de lung gi rgya mtsho chen por 'bab//'jug sgo gsum gyi mthar rgyas 'chad byed lung gi
chos kun snying po'i mdzod//log rtog tshig 'bru phye mar

thag byed thal ngag dbang po'i rdo rje 'bar//byams pa'i chos lnga'i nges don rab gsal byams chos lam gyi bang rim las//nye bar 'dzegs nas brgyud pa'i bsti gnas dga' ldan bgrod
pa'i lam sgo phye//dbu ma'i byung tshul yid bzhin lhun po rtsa 'jug TI ka lta khrid gnyis//lugs gnyis rnam 'byed dbu ma'i nges gsang gsal bar 'char byed stong mthun gnyis//gzhan
gzhung nor ba grangs su bgrang byas dngos gnas gsal ba sgo brgya pa//nges don bdud rtsi'i thigs pa mchog de tshangs dbyangs 'khor lo phyogs bcur sgrog/nyi zla'i
shing rtas legs par drangs pa'i bslab gnas 'chad byed rgyas bsdus dag/gzhi gsum phyag bzhes bdud rtsi'i gsos kyis 'dul ba'i bstan pa'i srog nas bzung//rnal 'byor spyod
gzhung rgya mtsho'i rlabs 'phreng bye brag bshad pa'i rgya mtshor 'khyil//sdom gsum nges gnas gsal byed sgron mes dpyod ldan mig gi dga' ston spel//zhes zur gyis mtshan
smos pa'i phar phyin theg pa dang rjes 'brel shog bu mda' tshad bzhugs lnga brgya ma'i glegs bam bcu gnyis/ mdo sngags spel ma'i dbus pa gdong 'don pod grangs bzhi/ bstod
tshogs chab shog la sa skya gras kyi po ti gnyis te pod grangs bco brgyad po gting skyes chos rje sku mched rnam pa gsum gyis re re phyag bzhengs gnang zhing bdag gir gnang
ba ni bka' drin zla med pa'i bstan pa'i khur bsnams par snang zhing/ bdag gis kyang 'bad nas de dag gi lung legs par thob bo//der dngul gdung gi las ka yang mthar phyin
nas sku gdung yid bzhin nor bu dbang gi rgyal po nyid kyang spyan drangs te sngon bkas bcad pa'i dgongs dbyings bzhin du bzhugs su gsol zhing/ chab ser las

bsgrubs pa'i ston pa 'jam dbyangs/ byams pa rnams kyi bar sku stong rwa re btab pa yang sku gdung gi mthar gser dngul gyi na bza' dang bcas pa bzhugs shing/ gzhan gzungs dang/
sangs rgyas kyi ring srel sogs nang bzhugs dpag tu med pa dang/ sngar bka'i rjes gnang mdzad pa'i lugs ltar rten li ma khyad par 'phags pa dag kyang bkra shis sgo mangs
kyi sgo so so ba dag tu bkod cing/ lhag par bal po ma Ni pA las bal po nyid nas bsgrubs te/ spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal phyag stong dang lhan cig phul ba'i bde mchog
zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa bal 'bum sde na legs grags chod pa de dngul gdung gi bum sgo'i thad che chung gi sgor bzhugs su gsol/ der thugs sras zhal slob rnams kyis rab
gnas brtan bzhugs kyang phul/ sa skyong chen po mi'i dbang po khu dbon blon 'bangs dang bcas pas kyang bkra shis dga' ston rgya cher spel zhes yongs su grags so//gang gi
'phrin las srid pa ji srid pa//mi nyams lhag par spel ba'i phan dgongs can//paN chen zhal las gdams pa'i chab rgyun gyis//yongs smin khyod thugs rjes sprul 'phags pa'i
tshogs//gting skyes pakun dga' rgyal mtshan chos kyi khri la bzhugs//brag dmar bakun dga' tshe 'phel zab chos 'khor lo bsgyur//glo bo pablo gros rgyal mtshan chos kyi rje
bo'i tshul//gu ge parnam rgyal dpal bzang cho rigs btsun pa'i ngang//mi nyagchos grags dpal bzang che dgu'i gtsug na mtho//tshal parin chen rgyal mtshan mkhas btsun bzang
por grags//phra phu basangs rgyas bzang po rigs pa smra ba'i mchog//khang gsar grwa tshang gimkhas pa mgar tsha phyogs kyi blo gsal skyong//slob dpon lalha yi btsun pa
nyid kyi thugs mtshor thim//slob dpon nyang ram palhun grub dpal bzang grub spyod lhug par ston//slob dpon nangs pasangs rgyas blo gros rigs pa'i ral gri 'phyar//snar thang
slob dpongrags pa bzang po mngon

pa'i sde snod 'dzin//brag dkar babsod nams rgyal mtshan yongs kyis srid zhu'i dang//gser gling pa Van der Kuijp: gringskun dga' bkra shis sgyu lus rmi lam 'byongs//glang thang
grub rgyal bangag dbang chos rgyal spyan snga'i mtshan dkar zhes//rje dbon shAka rgyan nges med chos la dges//pu rangs pakhra char mkhan po zhi dul mthong bas mdzes//glo
bo pabyams gling mkhan po smra ba mkhas pa'i mchog//glo bo pabrag dkar mkhan po nyid la dad pa'i phul//mnga' ris phyirdbu legs mkhan po lugs gnyis pha mthar son//rje
btsunkun dga' mchog grub stong nyid snying rje'i sku//spyang lung pagzhon nu chos grub dman 'gro yongs la brtse//pu rangs chos grub pablo gros rnam rgyal thugs rje che ldan
pa//glo bo kar ga Van der Kuijp: ka rag pashes rab dpal 'byor snying rje'i nyams kyis myos//kun dga' bzang pornal 'byor dbus smyon grub pa'i sa la bzhugs//bsod nams rgyal?dbu
legs grub chen nyams rtogs mngon du gyur//'phan yul padga' mo chos mdzad rtogs pa'i don rgyud 'dzin//thog? lungnam mkha' rab gsal bsgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzugs//mkhar
rtse lcang ra bablo gros bzang po rig pa'i ngar sgra sgrog/nyang stod rtse chen pardo rje rgyal po skad gnyis zung sbyor ngoms//mnga' ris glo bo padon yod grub pa
gzhung tshig blo nas bshor//phu 'byung paye shes lhun grub gdan sa'i las gter 'dzin//mar dgar ba (or: mang dkar ba?)rab gsal zla mgon dbang brgya'i phrin bsgyur mkhan//mus
pathugs rje dpal ba bzlas brjod dag la brtson//mus ram padkon mchogs grags pa chos sgo sna tshogs 'chad//bsam grub rtse parin chen bkra shis rigs ldan chos brgyud spel//phu
chung ka bcu padkon mchog rgyal mtshan 'phrin las mkha' dang mnyam//snar thang mkhan poshes rab dpal ldan gnas brtan sprul par grags//ra mo che payon tan chos 'phel
dbu tshad sbyangs pa'i dpe//sde bdun padbang phyug rgyal mtshan phrin las dar rgyas che//chu ba dus pasangs rgyas 'od zer 'chad nyan ngang la gshegs//phyogs las rnam rgyal
bstan phyir 'od zhur yal//rdo ring kun spangs chos skyong bran du 'khol//glo bo padbang phyug dpal bas rnam sras 'khor bcas gzigs//'phrang Kuijp: 'phrar po seng ge sgang
para ba mdo pas tshogs bdag

las la 'khol//sde pa sgar padon yod rdo rjes ku ru ku lle 'grub//shAkya rgyal mtshan'khon gyi gdung brgyud mkha' dbyings nyi ltar gsal//mkhan chen blo brtan pa/ mkhan chen
lhun grub bkra shis/ mkhan chen legs pa rin chen/ mkhan chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rin po che bkra shis rnam rgyal te mkhan rabs
drug/tshogs pa'i mkhan brgyud gser ri'i phreng ltar bsgrigs//gling smad mkhan po kun dga' dag dpal 'byor sogs/gzur gnas mkhas slob phyogs bcu'i rgyu skar 'dra//che dgu'i
bu slob bstod tshig rnga chen sgrog/mtshan smos pa 'di dag ni mtshon byed tsam ste/ gang gi zhal slob/ yang slob rjes 'jug/ brgyud 'dzin dang bcas pa ji srid sangs rgyas
kyi bstan pa'i rgyun dang lhan cig phrin las mchog gi bya ba chad pa med par chu'i rgyun lta bur gyur pa nyid do//zhes paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs
pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam par 'byed pa las/ phrin las kyi 'khor lo rgyun mi chad pa'i skabs las rjes su bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa nyi shu rtsa drug
pa'o// //Chapter 27: yongs su rdzogs pa'i skabsde ltar rnam thar snga ma gsum gdan bkod du byas ma zlos shing/ gang ma tshang ba'i thad khol du kha skong bgyis/ rang res
'bad rtsol drag pos paN chen nyid kyi zhabs la gtugs shing/ gsung gi bdud rtsi dngos su bzhes pa'i slob ma'i mchog bcu gnyis/ yang slob brgyud pa 'dzin pa bzhi ste/ dge
ba'i bshes gnyen bcu drug gi drung du gang las brgyud pa'i dbang lung gdams pa'i sgo/ chos kyi rgyal po'i dpal gyi mgur las bka' stsal ba phal cher thob cing/ de skabs re
re nas kyang rnam thar gyi zur mi 'dra ba'i cha phra ba thos pa kun kyang ma brjed par blo la gzungs su bsten pa dag so sor bkod/ dgung lo brgyad cu'i bar la hor kongs
med cing dbu zhabs gtan ma log pa/ rgyu skar 'char ba'i

go rim ltar bris pa 'di yongs su rdzogs par grub pa'o// //paN chen nyin byed dga' ldan nub ri'i rtser//dgongs pa bskyod po srin bu me khyer bdag//ma las btsas pas skal med
bdag gi migkhyed sku mthong ba'i yul du ma gyur grang//dad pa'i slong mos thos ldan phyug po'i sgor//lo rgyus zas kyi rnyed pa bslangs pa'i cha//rna ba'i snod du cung zad
chags pa dag/gdung shugs bkres pa'i nyams kyis gces par bzung//grog mkhar sbrang rtsi dpe bzhin phra ba'i dngos//rdul phran ma 'dres bsags pa'i tshig sbyor 'di//cha shas
yongs su gang ba'i zla ba ste//rnam thar yongs kyi tshig don ku muta phye//shin tu blo dman nyams chung bung ba'i rtsal//rnam dpyod gshog sgrog bskyod pa'i stobs zhan yang//rnam
thar pad tshal rgyu ba'i rkang drug bdag/lo rgyus sbrang rtsi'i bcud kyis lhag par tshim//gang yang rang gi bla ma'i rnam thar rang rang mos dad 'dren byed gang//gang
yang mdzad pa'i legs byas rgya chen rgya mtsho'i nor bu nor mchog gang//gang yang brjod pas zad par mi nus mi zad gter gyi bum bzang gang//gang yang bsngags 'os yon
tan rgyan phreng snyan tshig phreng du dngar ba gang//'di ltar dam pa'i mdzad pa'i cha//legs brjod bsod nams gzugs mchis na//lhun po'i spo las yongs rgal te//gling bzhi'i
khyon du tshud pa min//phal tshig dkyus su bris pa dag/blo dman skye bos go ched de//ma bsdams blun ngor brjod pa na//smra po rang nyid phyugs dang mtshungs//snyan ngag
sdebs legs mngon brjod lang tsho ma//rig gnas mkhyen pa'i yid kyi 'dod 'jo ba//rnar snyan brjod tshig rab gtsang dag pa'i ngag//mkhas mang yid kyi shing rta 'dren byed yin//tshig
grogs ma nyams don bzang

ljen pa can//smra ba po gang blun po las 'das mod//yi ge'i snang ba spro byed rmongs pa bdag//nam yang rang nyams mkhas pa'i khengs pa bral//cung zad las dkar dag pas yid bskul
nas//chos phyir dka' ba'i khur bskyed phyogs mtha' nyul//rnyed grags khyad gsad khyod zhabs bsten pa'i bshes//gang dag zhal sgor dbang lung gdams pa nod//phyogs med
phyogs bral phyogs 'dzin btang ba'i blo//phyogs mthong phyogs gcig smra ba'i phyogs byol nas//phyogs bcu phyogs kyi bshes gnyen phyogs gtogs la//phyogs tsam phyogs mtshungs
phyogs las rnam par rgyal//khyod kyi gsung gi zegs ma phra mo yang//khyod la rjes bsams 'bad pas legs btsal te//khyod kyi rjes slob yongs la phan bskyed phyir//khyod kyi
bstan pa'i khur chen snying nas blangs//kye ma snyigs ma'i dbang gyur pas//rang blos gzhal nas klan ka sgrog/phyogs 'dzin rab rib mig ldongs pas//ji bzhin mthong ba'i
yul ma gyur//'di na gya tshom spyod pa'i 'gros can 'jig rten las snang mchor chas mkhan//chos ltar bcos pa'i tshul gyis rab dregs tshigs sgras bstan pa 'dzin brtson zhing//bslab
gsum rgyan gyis chog par mi 'dzin 'bad pa'i las ro ba//bstan pa'i mig rkyen dman par gyur gang snying nas snying rje'i yul nyid lags//shAkya'i bstan 'dzin mchog 'di'i
dgongs pa'i dbyings//tshul ldan mang thos spong ba lhur len pa//rab dul zhi zhing gsong por smra ba can//chos brgyad bral gang khyod kyi rjes slob yin//yongs rdzogs
bstan pa'i gzhung lugs ma lus pa//gzigs pa rgya chen rang gzhan ma 'dres phyed//lung rigs dag pa'i sgron ma 'dzin pa can//

klog pa po de khyod kyis bsngags pa'i yul//nges 'byung yid can ngur smrig gos can dag/ri dgas dman pa ji bzhin pas mthar gnas//'tsho ba dag cing ci yang med 'chang ba'i//spong
ba pa des khyod kyi zhabs pad bsten//mdo dang tshig don zung 'brel 'chad pa'i ngag/khungs ldan brgyud pa'i srol brgya 'byed mkhas pa'i//chos 'khor so so'i grangs nges
ma 'dres par//legs rtogs gang de khyod kyi bstan 'dzin yin//de ltar yang yang rjes las gang brtsams nas//mang du brjod la dge tshogs ci mchis pas//mtha' yas 'gro ba'i las
sgrib kun sbyangs nas//chos kyi rgyal po khyod dang mtshungs gyur cig//ces paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo gros kyi rnam par thar pa zhib mo rnam
par 'byed palas/ yongs su rdzogs pa'i skabs las bsgrags pa'i rab tu byed pa nyer bdun pa'o// //Colophonde ltar paN chen rin po che'i sku che ba'i yon tan zhib mor bris
pa'i rab byed nyer bdun pa 'di yang ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gsum pa kha che paN chen shAkya shrI'i gdan seng ge'i khri la mngon par rab tu mtho ba/ skye med rang gsal chos
dbyings gdod ma'i mgon po mngon sum du gzigs pa'i mkhan chen rin po che'i zhal snga nas kyis bkas bskul ba'i dbang las/ snyoms las kyi bgyi ba cung zhig bsal te/ gang
gi bka' mi 'gog pa'i slad du/ grol mchog gis yi ger bkod pa 'dis/ bdag sogs sems can thams cad rgyal ba'i bstan pa'i gzhung lam la rjes su 'jug pa'i skal ba mchog dang ldan
par gyur cig/manggalaM bha wantu//shu bhaM//
